
-----title
泰安（奉符） (出生地)
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='503d4a0c4f794ebe87e0bf075ec76d40_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("503d4a0c4f794ebe87e0bf075ec76d40");'><span id='503d4a0c4f794ebe87e0bf075ec76d40_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1028')">1005-1028年</a>，1-24岁</div><div id='503d4a0c4f794ebe87e0bf075ec76d40' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1005&endYear=1005')">1005年</a>　生于山东泰安。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1006&endYear=1011')">1006-1011年</a>　居乡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1012&endYear=1012')">1012年</a>　父石丙进士及第。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1013&endYear=1013')">1013年</a>　居乡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1014&endYear=1014')">1014年</a>　丧母。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1015&endYear=1027')">1015-1027年</a>　居乡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1028&endYear=1028')">1028年</a>　不详。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='96d63a51c4ce4e6e96e57e9820fac685_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("96d63a51c4ce4e6e96e57e9820fac685");'><span id='96d63a51c4ce4e6e96e57e9820fac685_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1042')">1039-1042年</a>，35-38岁</div><div id='96d63a51c4ce4e6e96e57e9820fac685' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　在母丧戚中。躬耕徂徕山下，以《易》教授于家。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年4月27日</a>　四月二十七日，致书徐州知府张弇，言父丙不堪蜀道之远，求别择佚泰之地而安乐之。作品：《上徐州张刑部书》<div id='poem_1159698' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159698' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159698?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上徐州张刑部书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年4月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_1159698")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159698_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159698'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159698'>四月二十七日，哀子石介以在丧戚中，言不能文，谨直书情恳，顿首再拜于知府刑部阁下：介生十年，失母氏之爱，继以两母，今皆何恃，而所怙者独父，常自痛不能报三母劬劳鞠育之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159698_comment'></div>今父实老，而家贫，族累重，赖禄廪为养生之资，未得还所掌于君，退休于家，犹烦劳于官职之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159698_comment'></div>有子壮且仕于州县，进无才能取大官美禄以为尊亲显荣，退无智力谋丰资馀粟以供朝夕甘旨，使其亲老而不得佚，既不才也，又不孝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159698_comment'></div>今复有重于此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159698_comment'></div>大人景祐三年九月，用京东提点刑狱耿承制从政、审刑详议刘殿丞京、知齐州李职方逊、通判齐州王虞部鲰、通判明州吕虞部日新举状，改大理寺丞、知单州砀山县事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159698_comment'></div>审官循国朝之制，就徙于蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159698_comment'></div>蜀道之难，从来旧矣，少健轻捷者犹且疲乏弗克胜，岂老者所堪任也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159698_comment'></div>为人子既不才，又不孝，使父老不得休佚，复将如是而苦之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159698_comment'></div>若然，生子安用乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159698_comment'></div>是畜犬马之不若也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159698_comment'></div>犬马犹能吠乘，为其子反无所能，不若犬马哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159698_comment'></div>介少读六经，知尊君事父，臣子忠孝之大节，不能远希古人，窃自比于犬马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159698_comment'></div>故去年请于吏部，得蜀嘉州一官，以免大人之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159698_comment'></div>抵嘉仅月，母氏讣至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159698_comment'></div>本免大人之行者，以介故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159698_comment'></div>今介解官来，大人故又不得免其行矣，重介不才不孝之罪矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159698_comment'></div>然犬马之心，终不已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159698_comment'></div>遂请于上，愿俟终制复行，以免大人之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159698_comment'></div>状上而既不得报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159698_comment'></div>且大人齿衰，而蜀道远，又不可卒行，乃别择佚泰之地而求安乐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159698_comment'></div>徐在东夏为近辅，处列藩，为大府，通江、淮之运，来吴、楚之货，又为会津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159698_comment'></div>而癋土膏地润，足蒲鱼，宜稻菱，实为乐土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159698_comment'></div>今闻阁下以王府之迩臣、台阁之宿望，镇抚绥养，为土守长，尚清净，崇俭约，事不挠，民不烦，吏得守其司，官得安其职，斯可谓佚泰之地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159698_comment'></div>为人之子，得置其亲于佚泰之地，寝处安矣，食味嘉矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159698_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159698_comment'></div>木依于山，鱼依于渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159698_comment'></div>山有珀壑之深、云雾之润，木诚得其养矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159698_comment'></div>渊有潭府之奥、蒲藻之美，鱼诚得其所矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159698_comment'></div>茍斧斤不以时入山林，罔罟不以时入川泽，木得生乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159698_comment'></div>鱼得安乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159698_comment'></div>岂不系于仁政乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159698_comment'></div>今徐虽为近辅大府，会津乐土，夫欲求佚泰其亲、安乐其亲，岂不系于阁下乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159698_comment'></div>仁政之广，及于草木鱼鸟，癋人之亲焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159698_comment'></div>介知寝处安矣，食味嘉矣，不胜人子诃诃之诚，伏惟阁下哀怜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159698_comment'></div>不次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159698_comment'></div>介再拜<span class='inlineComment2'>（《徂徕石先生全集》卷一六。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159698_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1159698'>「解官来」三字原缺，据张本补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159698_comment'></div>石本、库本作「解来」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1159698_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年5月</a>　谒李迪于府中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　冬，致书李迪，感激其衣食之德。李迪曾至泰山拜访孙复，见孙复年四十未娶，以弟之女妻之。介作《贤李》赞之。作品：《谢兖州李相公启
，《贤李》<div id='poem_1159710' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159710' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159710?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢兖州李相公启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_1159710")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159710_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159710'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159710'>介顿首百拜资政相公阁下：孟冬渐寒，伏惟台候万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159710_comment'></div>介五月中过府中，得获参觐，伏蒙相公恩遇如常，介不胜感铭之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159710_comment'></div>恭以相公之德，兖州之人衣食之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159710_comment'></div>衣食之厚且足，无如介者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159710_comment'></div>生景德之乙巳岁，介生之年，相公为状元，由大匠丞通判于兖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159710_comment'></div>逮今三十五年，相公凡四来，其殖衣食于兖州也，富且饶矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159710_comment'></div>自相公初殖之，介则衣食之，介今生三十五年，衣食相公三十五年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159710_comment'></div>先介一年生者，衣食多于介一年，后介一年生者，衣食少于介一年，何癋有先四十年、五十年生者，后三十年、四十年生者，是兖州之人衣食相公无如介厚且足者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159710_comment'></div>介于兖州之人衣食相公最厚，兖州于天下衣食相公又厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159710_comment'></div>盖相公来兖州四矣，陶宰天下再矣，故衣食之有厚薄焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159710_comment'></div>旦暮相公三正台席，推兖州衣食以及天下，天下衣食相公其亦如兖州之人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159710_comment'></div>夫衣食乎天下，福德爵禄宁有穷时乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159710_comment'></div>伏惟相公倍加慎重。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1159710_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年12月</a>　十二月，孔道辅卒。作《祭孔中丞》，赞其至忠至诚之道。<div id='poem_1159808' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159808' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159808?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭孔中丞文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_1159808")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159808_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159808'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159808'>昔公为谏议大夫、知兖州，臣僚有以诗千篇献上者，执政者即请进为龙图阁直学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159808_comment'></div>上曰：「千首诗，岂若孔某一言」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159808_comment'></div>即日拜龙图阁直学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159808_comment'></div>公再为中丞，风格益峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159808_comment'></div>及公没，刘平战死于阵，谗贼害忠良，诬奏平非战屈，乃叛耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159808_comment'></div>天子怒，将夷平家，平家胥靡就阙，魾号道途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159808_comment'></div>逢驺唱中丞来，平家将扣中丞马言其事，两街卖贩儿以数千，叹曰：「徒往诉耳，是非孔中丞者」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159808_comment'></div>平家恸哭而止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159808_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159808_comment'></div>至尊极者君，至愚暗者民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159808_comment'></div>尊极则不信，愚暗则难开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159808_comment'></div>非公至忠，岂能动尊极耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159808_comment'></div>非公至诚，岂能感愚暗耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159808_comment'></div>动乎尊极，感乎愚暗，公之道格乎上下矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159808_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159808_comment'></div>公之生也，君称之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159808_comment'></div>公之死也，人感之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159808_comment'></div>公之道全于死生矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159808_comment'></div>夫道格于上下为著，全于死生为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159808_comment'></div>举是二节，公之道充于天地之间矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159808_comment'></div>大冬残鱀，风号云咽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159808_comment'></div>节物惨淡，心肝摧折。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159808_comment'></div>炉烟氤氲，樽酒冷烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159808_comment'></div>享诚不享味，公来降兹。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1159808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1159808'><span class='label'>按：</span>《皇朝文炮》卷一三二。又见《文章辨体汇选》卷七五九，《三续古文奇赏》卷二六，陈校本附录佚文。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1159808_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　青州州学扩充完成，应邀题于壁，作《青州州学公用记》<div id='poem_1159793' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159793' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159793?labeling=true' target='_blank'>青州州学公田记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_1159793")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159793_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159793'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159793'>故仆射相国沂公，初作青州学成，奏天子，天子赐学名，且颁公田三十顷，次入于学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159793_comment'></div>公患田少不足，又傍学作屋百二十间，岁入于学钱三十一万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159793_comment'></div>逮今十稔，学益兴而士倍多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159793_comment'></div>太守赵集贤广公之意，取南城隙地，又作屋八十三室，别为钩盾六十二间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159793_comment'></div>岁入于学，通六十七万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159793_comment'></div>学之公用，于是大充，而养士之道称矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159793_comment'></div>学官与诸弟子侈之，请记于壁，曰：立其法万世不改者，道之本也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159793_comment'></div>通其变使民不倦者，道之中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159793_comment'></div>本，故万世不易也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159793_comment'></div>中，故万世可行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159793_comment'></div>若伏羲、神农、黄帝、尧、舜氏树君臣、父子、上下之制，立其法，万世不改者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159793_comment'></div>是之谓本焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159793_comment'></div>服牛乘马，上栋下宇，弧矢网罟之宜，舟楫耒耜之利，棺睳之便，臼杵之用，通其变，使民不倦者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159793_comment'></div>是之谓中焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159793_comment'></div>相国沿三代明王之作，取古者家有塾、党有庠、术有序、国有学之制，建学于青，立其本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159793_comment'></div>集贤申《易·大畜》「养贤」、《颐》「养正《、」需》「饬食晏乐」、《兑》「朋友讲习」之义，立宽于学，制其中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159793_comment'></div>大凡舒则人暇，局则人困，故善教者优游而至道，不善教者急速而强人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159793_comment'></div>其要贵夫劳逸之节焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159793_comment'></div>《礼》曰：「张而不弛，文、武不为也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159793_comment'></div>一弛一张，文、武之道也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159793_comment'></div>今夫学者六艺经传千万言，以时而讽之，其为功博矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159793_comment'></div>仁义礼乐、忠信孝悌之道，天地阴阳、星辰灾变之动，以时而求之，其为业广矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159793_comment'></div>广博而难卒，勤苦而后能成，蚤起夜诵，寒暑不废，衣冠不解，则是常张之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159793_comment'></div>岁有田，日有秩，劳有休，怠有养，所以息焉、游焉，是一张一弛之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159793_comment'></div>君子谓相国、集贤善教矣，张而不急，弛而不废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159793_comment'></div>初，集贤乐学之经始甚亟，乃择材吏，得节度推官蔡君蚮，用董其役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159793_comment'></div>作屋若钩盾百四十五间，而取材于县官之馀，借力于公家之隙，不烦于府，不扰于民，和说而以成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159793_comment'></div>予谓相国善作也，集贤善述也，蔡君善卒相国、集贤之志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159793_comment'></div>见皏斯文，既不得让，因记其岁月云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1159793_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　感叹文之不复，道之不见。作品：《上张兵部书》<div id='poem_1159670' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159670' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159670?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上张兵部书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_1159670")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159670_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159670'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159670'>介尝读《易》，至《序卦》曰：「剥者，剥也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159670_comment'></div>物不可以终尽，故受之以复」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159670_comment'></div>斯文也，剥且三十年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159670_comment'></div>剥之将尽，其党朋进不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159670_comment'></div>昔尧、舜、禹之道剥于癸，天受之汤，尧、舜、禹之道复；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159670_comment'></div>汤之道剥于受，天受之文、武、周公，汤之道复；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159670_comment'></div>文、武、周公之道剥于幽、厉，天受之孔子，文、武、周公之道复；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159670_comment'></div>孔子之道始剥于杨、墨，中剥于庄、韩，又剥于秦、莽，又剥于晋、宋、齐、梁、陈五代，终剥于佛、老，天受之孟轲、荀卿、扬雄、王通、韩愈，孔子之道复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159670_comment'></div>今斯文也，剥已极矣，而不复，天岂遂丧斯文哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159670_comment'></div>斯文丧，则尧、舜、禹、汤、周公、孔子之道不可见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159670_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159670_comment'></div>小子不肖，然每至于斯，未尝不流涕横席，终夜不寐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159670_comment'></div>顾己无孟轲、荀卿、扬雄、文中子、吏部之力，不能亟复斯文，其心亦不敢须臾忘此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159670_comment'></div>惟执事怜之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159670_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159670_comment'></div>介顿首。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1159670_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　送友人赴任。作品：《送冯司理之任彭州》<div id='poem_83262' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_83262' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/83262?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送冯司理之任彭州</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_83262")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_83262_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_83262'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_83262'>李白诗中蜀道难，把诗试读泪汍澜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_83262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_83262'>江形诘曲千回折，岭路崚嶒万屈盘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_83262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_83262'>登陟去年腰仅折，追思今日鼻犹酸<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：予去年罢嘉州归。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_83262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_83262'>此行君不同屯蹇，五马相知旧长官<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：彭牧与君常同官。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_83262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_83262'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_83262_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　在母丧戚中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　致书徐州扈谏议，求其照顾石丙。作品：《上徐州扈谏议》<div id='poem_1159702' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159702' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159702?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上徐州扈谏议书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1040年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_1159702")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159702_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159702'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159702'>知府谏议阁下：夫父道也者，君道也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159702_comment'></div>君道也者，乾道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159702_comment'></div>首万物者乾，则以君癋焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159702_comment'></div>尊万邦者君，则以父拟焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159702_comment'></div>盖君也者，天下之达贵也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159702_comment'></div>父也者，天下之达亲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159702_comment'></div>贵，故天下慕之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159702_comment'></div>亲，故天下爱之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159702_comment'></div>一国之内足慕者，君也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159702_comment'></div>一家之内足爱者，亲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159702_comment'></div>是以人臣以近君为荣，人子以事亲为乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159702_comment'></div>夫一日三接，便蕃宠锡，孰荣如之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159702_comment'></div>朝夕左右，承顺颜色，孰乐如之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159702_comment'></div>然内外之事不可一也，出入之任不可择也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159702_comment'></div>入以奉谋猷，出以守疆埸，臣之义也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159702_comment'></div>内以调甘旨，外以服勤劳，子之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159702_comment'></div>内者盖不可以守疆埸为惮，而忠臣忧君之志以为苦也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159702_comment'></div>外者盖不可以服勤劳为辞，而孝子念亲之心以为伤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159702_comment'></div>大人七十有一岁矣，而以五代未葬，卜后年辛巳吉，凡衣衾棺睳之具，待禄而后办，未能遂归林泉以取休佚，犹独僶俛于官职之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159702_comment'></div>且大人既老矣，介则当晨昏定省，日亲上食，谨视寒眗之节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159702_comment'></div>而乃远违几杖，亏一日三至寝门之礼，人子之义，得无阙乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159702_comment'></div>诚罪人矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159702_comment'></div>诚罪人矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159702_comment'></div>然前所谓内以调甘旨，外以服勤劳，盖亦不得而惮也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159702_comment'></div>介家四十口，曾、高以来，耕田为业，田薄牛弱，常苦贫窭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159702_comment'></div>岁尽天之时，穷地之利，竭人之力，并大人与介两人禄，四十口仅得饱食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159702_comment'></div>今介禄阙，大人独食不足，乃泣别庭闱，远来田园，学老圃老农之事，勤稼树桑，庶几四十口衣夫帛、食夫粟，而免寒馁之忧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159702_comment'></div>事不两遂，不得朝夕左右，承顺颜色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159702_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159702_comment'></div>前年去蜀五千里，今又在此，其孝子念亲之心，亦可怜矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159702_comment'></div>恭惟阁下辍七人之近列，开千里之大邦，惟此徐方，蒙受其福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159702_comment'></div>《语》曰：「老者安之，少者怀之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159702_comment'></div>阁下之福，施之必有先后之次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159702_comment'></div>以大人，可称为老者矣，则受阁下之福，宜在先矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159702_comment'></div>用是，将有以释孝子念亲之心一二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159702_comment'></div>瞻望门戟，不胜欢忭欣跃之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159702_comment'></div>介顿首再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1159702_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年3月</a>　三月，父丙卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年7月18日</a>　作《泰山书院记》，比孙复如孟子，韩愈。尊其为“泰山先生”。<div id='poem_1159792' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159792' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159792?labeling=true' target='_blank'>泰山书院记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1040年7月18日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_1159792")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159792_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159792'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159792'>自周以上观之，贤人之达者，皋陶、傅说、伊尹、吕望、召公、毕公是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159792_comment'></div>自周以下观之，贤人之穷者，孟子、扬子、文中子、吏部是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159792_comment'></div>然较其功业德行，穷不必易达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159792_comment'></div>吏部后三百年，贤人之穷者，又有泰山先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159792_comment'></div>孟子、扬子、文中子、吏部皆以其道授弟子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159792_comment'></div>既授弟子，复传之于书，其书大行，其道大耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159792_comment'></div>先生亦以其道授弟子，既授之弟子，亦将传之于书，将使其书大行，其道大耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159792_comment'></div>乃于泰山之阳起学舍，构堂，聚先圣之书满屋，与群弟子而居之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159792_comment'></div>当时游从之贵者，孟子则有梁惠王、齐宣王、滕文公之属，扬子则有刘歆、桓谭之属，文中子则有越公之属，吏部则有裴晋公、郑相国、张仆射之属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159792_comment'></div>门人之高第者，孟则有万章、公孙丑、乐克之徒，扬则有侯芭、刘盏之徒，文中子则有董常、程元、薛收、李靖、杜如晦、房、魏之徒，吏部则有李观、李翱、李汉、张籍、皇甫卜之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159792_comment'></div>今先生游从之贵者，故王沂公、蔡贰卿、李秦州，孔中丞，今李丞相、范经略、明子京、张安道、士熙道、祖择之，门人之高第者，石介、刘牧、姜睶、张洞、李鄈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159792_comment'></div>足以相望于千百年之间矣，孰谓先生穷乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159792_comment'></div>大哉，圣贤之道无屯泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159792_comment'></div>孟子、扬子、文中子、吏部皆屯于无位与小官，而孟子泰于七篇，扬子泰于《法言》、《太玄》，文中子泰于续经、《中说》，吏部泰于《原道》、《论佛骨表》十馀万言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159792_comment'></div>先生尝以尽孔子之心者大《易》，尽孔子之用者《春秋》，是二大经，圣人之极笔也，治世之大法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159792_comment'></div>故作《易说》六十四篇，《春秋尊王发微》十七卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159792_comment'></div>疑四凶之不去，十六相之不举，故作《尧权》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159792_comment'></div>防后世之篡夺，诸侯之僭翨，故作《舜制》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159792_comment'></div>辨注家之误，正世子之名，故作《正名解》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159792_comment'></div>美出处之得，明传嗣之嫡，故作《四皓论》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159792_comment'></div>先生述作，上宗周、孔，下拟韩、孟，是以为泰山先生，孰少之哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159792_comment'></div>介乐先生之道，大先生之为，请以此说刊之石，陷于讲堂之西壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159792_comment'></div>康定元年七月十八日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1159792_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年8月</a>　上书杜衍，推荐孙复。上书韩琦，范仲淹，推荐孙复，姜潜，张泂，李缊等。作品：《上杜副枢书》，《上韩密学经略使书》，《上范经略书》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　作书与祖无择，希其以己之势力救孙复之穷。作品：《与祖择之书》<div id='poem_1159687' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159687' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159687?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与祖择之书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1040年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_1159687")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159687_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159687'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159687'>济南通理廷尉评事足下：自周以上观之，圣人之穷者唯孔子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159687_comment'></div>自周以下观之，贤人之穷者唯泰山明复先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159687_comment'></div>自周以上圣人，若伏羲、黄帝、尧、舜、禹、汤、文王、武王，皆有天下，独孔子无位，身为旅人，聘七十国，卒不遇，乃遭厄陈、畏匡、削迹、伐树之困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159687_comment'></div>自周以下贤人，若孟轲，后车数十乘，从者数百人，以传食于诸侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159687_comment'></div>荀癋，三为祭酒，再为兰陵令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159687_comment'></div>扬雄，仕至执戟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159687_comment'></div>仲淹，河、汾之有田有庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159687_comment'></div>吏部，官登侍郎，立淮西功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159687_comment'></div>甚矣，独先生四十九岁，病卧山阿，衣弗充，食弗给，日抱《春秋》、《周易》读诵，探伏羲、文王、周公、孔子之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159687_comment'></div>上无斗升禄以养妻子，中无贤诸侯、名卿贤相以相慰荐，下无一夫之田，五亩之桑，以供伏腊，可谓穷矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159687_comment'></div>然孔子之穷，穷于无位，不穷于所以为孔子者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159687_comment'></div>先生之穷，穷于身而不穷乎道，乌得谓之穷乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159687_comment'></div>今夫衣弗充，食弗给，不足以逃饥寒之忧，而且再世未葬，亟谋襄事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159687_comment'></div>彼衣衾、棺睳不具，日夜涕泣，仰天悲嗟，此所谓先生之穷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159687_comment'></div>先生穷于身，而吾曹穷于势力，不能致先生于泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159687_comment'></div>择之以文章命世，登甲科，通理列郡，有富贵之基，公相之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159687_comment'></div>在吾曹间，择之若有势力者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159687_comment'></div>故敢以先生之穷告于择之，惟择之穷势力而后已，无使先生终否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159687_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159687_comment'></div>介再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1159687_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　丧戚中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年2月21日</a>　奉符民众就徂徕山下，求介救前奉符大夫马永伯之穷。时介亦在困顿中，无力解救，于是介作书与张安石，望其助之。作品：《与张安石书》<div id='poem_1159705' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159705' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159705?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与张安石书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年2月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_1159705")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159705_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159705'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159705'>岁庚辰十一月五日，奉符大夫马君永伯下吏，奉符民如赤子之失慈父母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159705_comment'></div>自十一月五日至二月十一日，凡百有六日，延颈引首，南望大夫之来，若在大暑思涤清风，若坐赤炭思濯寒波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159705_comment'></div>二十一日，大夫被免，民以千数，环立大哭，若以久馁方食而夺其辅，大寒始衣而劫其纩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159705_comment'></div>哭已，咸曰：「吾大夫奉身俭，行己廉，守法平，操心公，养民舒闲，约吏急速。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159705_comment'></div>自大夫来，吾曹安于里闾，晏眠饱食，老息壮作，不夺吾种殖之时，不害吾生养之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159705_comment'></div>经岁，村巷矱不惊，犬不吠，盗贼不入，吏胥不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159705_comment'></div>州县之政，赋税为急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159705_comment'></div>邻县督责烦数，敲扑之声相闻，里胥累累，系于道路，流血满令厅阶，犹出期不克办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159705_comment'></div>吾大夫但敛手坐席上，时召老叟至其前，与之相约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159705_comment'></div>所谓里胥者，皆放于田亩，严禁戒，不得与民相见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159705_comment'></div>不遣一吏走，不施一杖笞，常先期赋登数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159705_comment'></div>治吾邑者，育吾曹，可谓勤且至矣，可谓义且恩矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159705_comment'></div>吾曹在下观吾大夫，无丝发辜天负民，无分寸枉道欺心，而无罪免去，兹非吾大夫之不幸也，吾曹之不幸也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159705_comment'></div>于是相与环立，又哭且恸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159705_comment'></div>既而，又闻大夫无资不能行，尽货易其帷集之属乃能行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159705_comment'></div>虽能行，闻其寓鲁之西任城，无环堵之室，无一亩之田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159705_comment'></div>大夫及夫人、若女、若儿、若姨监皂隶十数口，衣不续而炊不继，朝诉饥而暮啼寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159705_comment'></div>吾大夫至此，吾曹德大夫甚深，忍坐视之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159705_comment'></div>乃群走队趋，就徂徕下绕石介泣告之曰：「吾曹尝闻昔田横能养士，当横之难，五百人死之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159705_comment'></div>今大夫之忧，幸未至横，吾曹亦未当从五百人者以死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159705_comment'></div>然吾大夫朝夕有饥寒之虑，吾曹民尔，无智力为营其衣食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159705_comment'></div>君在吾乡，号为有智力者，君宜念吾曹区区之心，图救吾大夫之穷」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159705_comment'></div>介闻之，大羞愧，且恻然悼之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159705_comment'></div>悼者，悼马大夫之窘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159705_comment'></div>愧者，愧此民之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159705_comment'></div>虽悼且愧，而方连遭大忧，在困踬憔悴中，旦暮自虞就死，何得锱铢势力解马大夫之忧，慰此民之勤勤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159705_comment'></div>然大夫之忧深矣，此民之勤勤至矣，皆义不可已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159705_comment'></div>安石读周、孔之书，知周、孔之道，富仁义之文，有仁义之心，岂不有意乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159705_comment'></div>介白。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1159705_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　门人杜默辞归，介作《三豪诗》送之，推石延年，欧阳修，杜默为诗，文，歌三豪。作品：《三豪诗送杜默师雄并序》<div id='poem_83229' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_83229' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/83229?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三豪诗送杜默师雄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_83229")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_83229_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_83229'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_83229'>曼卿豪于诗，社坛高数层。<div id='poem_sentence_0_83229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_83229'>永叔豪于辞，举世绝俦朋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_83229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_83229'>师雄歌亦豪，三人宜同称。<div id='poem_sentence_2_83229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_83229'>曼卿苦汩没，老死殿中丞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_83229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_83229'>身虽埋黄泉，诗名长如冰。<div id='poem_sentence_4_83229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_83229'>永叔亦<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_83229", 83229, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>连蹇</span>，病鸾方骞腾。<div id='poem_sentence_5_83229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_83229'>四海让独步，三馆最后登。<div id='poem_sentence_6_83229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_83229'>师雄二十二，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_83229", 83229, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>笔距</span>狞如鹰。<div id='poem_sentence_7_83229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_83229'>才格自天来，辞华非学能。<div id='poem_sentence_8_83229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_83229'>回顾李贺辈，粗俗良可憎。<div id='poem_sentence_9_83229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_83229'>玉川月蚀诗，犹欲相凭陵。<div id='poem_sentence_10_83229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_83229'>曼卿苟不死，其才堪股肱。<div id='poem_sentence_11_83229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_83229'>永叔器甚闳，用之王道兴。<div id='poem_sentence_12_83229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_83229'>师雄子勉旃，勿便生骄矜。<div id='poem_sentence_13_83229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_83229'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_83229_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年5月2日</a>　门人张绩，李常举进士，介醉之以酒，又赠之以言，以释相离之怀。五月二日作《送张绩李常序》<div id='poem_1159720' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159720' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159720?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送张绩李常序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年5月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_1159720")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159720_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159720'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159720'>孔子之大道，为异端侵害，不容于世实三千年，诸公能维而持之，不能排而去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159720_comment'></div>维之持之，道不绝矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159720_comment'></div>不去其害，道终病矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159720_comment'></div>韩文公所谓「不塞不流，不止不行」是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159720_comment'></div>予不自揆度，乃奋独力，直斥其人而攻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159720_comment'></div>我寡彼徒众，反攻予者日以千数，视予之肉，虎动吻而狼磨牙，赖圣君天覆地容，得免于祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159720_comment'></div>濮人张禹功、李遵道者，其居与予不相远，耳目接于予固熟，则宜其知予之所为如是，得祸如是，辄不惮直以身冒予之祸，来山中而助予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159720_comment'></div>扬子云称轲之勇，若禹功、遵道者，其勇者欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159720_comment'></div>太史正崔杼之罪，杀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159720_comment'></div>其弟又书，杼又杀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159720_comment'></div>南史闻之，执简以往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159720_comment'></div>太史初正杼之罪，知为史者，然犹未知必得诛于杼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159720_comment'></div>若南史闻已杀二人矣，又执简以往，是真不畏死者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159720_comment'></div>予攻害孔子者，予知为孔子者，然未知必得罪于害孔子之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159720_comment'></div>若禹功、遵道已见予之所得祸如是，又来助予，是真勇者矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159720_comment'></div>予今年三十七而发半白，然心益壮而气不衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159720_comment'></div>禹功少予十四岁，遵道少予十五岁，其文如进六军而作鼓者，严猛齐厉，张皇奋施，可式可畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159720_comment'></div>当与予周旋焉，达也以孔氏之道，穷也以孔氏之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159720_comment'></div>达而万物不通乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159720_comment'></div>穷而垂之于后世不明乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159720_comment'></div>穷达之间，绰然有馀裕，其有能动心乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159720_comment'></div>禹功藏用于神，其得天下之几欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159720_comment'></div>遵道直道而行，其明天下之治欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159720_comment'></div>几近《易》，治近《春秋》，二子之道，皆道也，与世不迂，其必达矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159720_comment'></div>去举进士，予醉之以酒，复赠之以言，以释相离之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159720_comment'></div>辛巳夏五月二日，石介序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1159720_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年7月</a>　祖无择罢济南将归，别孙复，石介于泰山，徂徕，相与讲经论道，举觞赋诗，五日后去。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年7月12日</a>　作《送祖择之序》<div id='poem_1159719' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159719' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159719?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送祖择之序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年7月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_1159719")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159719_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159719'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159719'>择之罢济南，将归阙，自历山南走三百里，别明复先生暨予于泰山、徂徕，相与讲道德，究经术，耽云霞，玩水石，举觞赋诗，五日而后去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159719_comment'></div>以所坐乘重为明复之寿，为予书先君之铭于石以为勒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159719_comment'></div>择之以文章登甲科，天下之望甚盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159719_comment'></div>不十年，当辅相天子，为宋大臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159719_comment'></div>为人资材已高，又自能知尧、舜、周、孔之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159719_comment'></div>顾明复与予，饥寒山谷中，何有毫发利于择之，而冒苦辛、倾肝胆予二人，岂有求邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159719_comment'></div>明复谓无以谢择之，发圣人之蕴，明王道之极，择之拜而受之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159719_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159719_comment'></div>《春秋》赏罚二百四十二年，至矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159719_comment'></div>仲尼之心，独拨衰周一世之乱反诸于正，十二经揭如日月，昭明于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159719_comment'></div>后之圣贤，得之多者帝，得之少者王，不得者霸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159719_comment'></div>明复之报，为不轻矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159719_comment'></div>予经学浅，不能希明复，然义不可嘿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159719_comment'></div>夫趋时，物之情也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159719_comment'></div>徇道，人之难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159719_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159719_comment'></div>诸侯交迎，倾国封之，枉尺直寻，吾死不为，见之孟轲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159719_comment'></div>寻、邑三公，舜、歆高爵，不作符命，甘投于阁，见之子云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159719_comment'></div>潮州八千，几死瘴眕，归来京兆，不肯婵娟，见之吏部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159719_comment'></div>嗟嗟李眅，徇主从昏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159719_comment'></div>咄咄宗元，附权邀官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159719_comment'></div>观而始节，岂为不完？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159719_comment'></div>弗能有终，至今痕瘢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159719_comment'></div>择之与予，说蕴深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159719_comment'></div>此去近天子，得与我相磨切天下是非，亦得时见上，讲道君政得失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159719_comment'></div>天子、宰相曰是，择之曰是，天子、宰相曰非，择之曰非，择之官日进而宠日深矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159719_comment'></div>天子、宰相曰是，择之曰非，天子、宰相曰非，择之曰是，择之前有鼎镬而后有盺钺矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159719_comment'></div>古之君子，辞官职而遗宠禄，趋鼎镬而就盺钺，非以官职宠禄为忧，而鼎镬盺钺为乐也，道适当然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159719_comment'></div>择之于道，安之者，非利而行之者，非畏罪而强之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159719_comment'></div>予所以云，姑为报之资尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159719_comment'></div>康定二年七月十二日序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1159719_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　上书王拱臣，言石氏自高祖以降至于六世孙七十丧，咸未改葬。求其拔介之穷，而成介之丧。作品：《上王状元书》<div id='poem_1159682' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159682' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159682?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上王状元书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_1159682")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159682_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159682'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159682'>状元舍人君贶执事：人在忧患，则哭号叫诉，以求恤于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159682_comment'></div>然忧患有缓急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159682_comment'></div>若夫坠而入井，非忧患也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159682_comment'></div>走而蹈于火，非忧患也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159682_comment'></div>陷于锋刃，值于寇乱，非忧患也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159682_comment'></div>罹于冻馁，窜于蛮荒，非忧患也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159682_comment'></div>没于河，溺于海，非忧患也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159682_comment'></div>覆于珀石，投于汤镬，非忧患也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159682_comment'></div>何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159682_comment'></div>夫入井、蹈火、锋刃、寇乱、冻馁、蛮荒、没河、溺海、珀石、汤镬，不过暴一身于死尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159682_comment'></div>自古皆有死，胡忧患之云哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159682_comment'></div>而乃哭号叫诉，以求恤于人，是茍避死已，丈夫羞为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159682_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159682_comment'></div>石氏自周、汉以来，至于吾宋之八十一年，百馀祀，自高祖以降至于六世孙七十丧，咸未改葬，此真可以谓之忧患矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159682_comment'></div>不哭号叫诉以求恤于人，则无以能济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159682_comment'></div>兹介所以数百里之外，声尽气绝而继之以泣，以告于执事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159682_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159682_comment'></div>诸侯五月、大夫三月、士逾月而葬，谓之礼经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159682_comment'></div>是故《春秋》讥缓葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159682_comment'></div>石氏之葬，可谓缓矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159682_comment'></div>先人三十年营之，迄于今年之八月，志未就而先人没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159682_comment'></div>当将终之时，制泪忍死，执介手以命于介。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159682_comment'></div>且曰：「汝不能成若翁之志，吾不瞑矣」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159682_comment'></div>故介自受命以来，十有七月矣，未尝敢一饭甘、一寝安、一衣暖、一饮乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159682_comment'></div>坐不敢正席，行不敢正履，终日战战视视，若怀冰炭，若负芒刺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159682_comment'></div>大惧坠先人之命，移天下不孝之罪，萃于厥躬，小子受谴于明，先人抱恨于幽，七十丧之魂无所依归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159682_comment'></div>是用今年八月，先人之吉岁嘉月也，以图襄事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159682_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159682_comment'></div>石氏自高、曾以来，以农名，家居东附徂徕，西倚汶，有故田三百亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159682_comment'></div>附徂徕者硗确，种不入；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159682_comment'></div>倚汶者虽肥坟，阅岁汶溢为害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159682_comment'></div>逢岁大有，穗不满三百石，食常不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159682_comment'></div>赖先人禄赐，介又幸有秩，姑逃于冻馁之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159682_comment'></div>先人没，禄赐绝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159682_comment'></div>介服丧，秩亦阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159682_comment'></div>专以田三百亩，衣食夫五十之口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159682_comment'></div>去年平原出水、蝗为灾，三百亩之田，不餍水，则饫蝗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159682_comment'></div>死者固不可忘，生者又不可不养，先人三十年营所葬之资，已为五十口衣食之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159682_comment'></div>今兹大事，当用五十万，不干于有道，终不克葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159682_comment'></div>尝闻昔代国公为太学生，家信至，寄钱四十万为学粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159682_comment'></div>有鄀服叫门云：「五代未葬」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159682_comment'></div>代公即命以车，一时载去，略无留者，亦不问姓氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159682_comment'></div>代公其年绝粮，不能成举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159682_comment'></div>柳河东布衣时，坐酒肆中，有书生在其侧，言贫无以葬，柳即搜于其家，得白金百馀两、钱数万遗之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159682_comment'></div>夫人皆有施也，施之宜，谓之义；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159682_comment'></div>夫人皆有恤也，恤之远，谓之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159682_comment'></div>二公之施，至于漏泉，可谓义矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1159682_comment'></div>二公之恤，及于枯骨，可谓仁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1159682_comment'></div>夫德莫大于仁义，德厚者流必远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1159682_comment'></div>故代公富贵功业，光隆于唐，河东文章声名，照映本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1159682_comment'></div>介今之穷，过于彼鄀服与书生者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1159682_comment'></div>执事能以代公、河东仁义，拔介之穷而成介之葬，执事之施，固不求报，而介德执事也，当如何焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1159682_comment'></div>惟执事念之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1159682_comment'></div>不次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1159682_comment'></div>介叩头泣血，再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_54_1159682_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年8月8日</a>　葬五世未葬者七十丧于徂徕西北，汶河东岸，作《石氏墓表》<div id='poem_1159807' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159807' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159807?labeling=true' target='_blank'>石氏墓志</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年8月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_1159807")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159807_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159807'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159807'>石氏之先出于卫康叔之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159807_comment'></div>康叔，文王之子，周公之母弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159807_comment'></div>然则石姬姓矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159807_comment'></div>按《本纪》云：「卫，静伯生公叔，公叔生显伯，显伯孙挚生何，为石氏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159807_comment'></div>《春秋左氏传》隐三年有石道，道子厚，庄十三年有石祈子，成四年有石稷，襄十七年、十九年有石买，二十七年、二十八年有石恶，襄二十八年、哀十七年有石圃，哀十三年有石曼姑，哀十五年有石乞，十七年有石圃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159807_comment'></div>《礼记·檀弓》注有石骀仲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159807_comment'></div>庄八年又有齐小臣石之纷如，十九年又有周士石速，僖三十年又有郑大夫石甲父，文十七年有石楚，成十年有石首，襄十一年、十三年有太宰石㚟，昭三十二年周又有石张，定十四年又有天子之士石尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159807_comment'></div>定十年又有宋卿石尤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159807_comment'></div>六国时有石奢，尝相楚国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159807_comment'></div>汉有万石君父子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159807_comment'></div>晋有石苞、石统、石乔、石崇、石朴，又有石炮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159807_comment'></div>唐有石抱忠，则天朝为天官侍郎，石雄为将，石演芬著忠义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159807_comment'></div>□六世祖自沧州乐陵县迁焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159807_comment'></div>今为兖州人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159807_comment'></div>吾祖初迁而南，得邑曰乾封<span class='inlineComment2'>（后改奉符，）</span>乡曰梁甫，里曰云亭，村曰商王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159807_comment'></div>负泰山，挟徂徕，有二大山之镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159807_comment'></div>且汶水注其后，经其西，遂筑居焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159807_comment'></div>「仁者乐山，智者乐水」，吾祖其近仁智者欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159807_comment'></div>吾祖之初来，既鲜兄弟，亦无族姻，有田百亩，专以农为业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159807_comment'></div>久之，始生高祖逵，高祖乃生曾祖七人，石氏于是遂蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159807_comment'></div>长曾祖性严毅，善于治家，每晨起，令劄子弟毕，先趋田亩，群子弟无敢后者，故石氏富于粟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159807_comment'></div>且当五代兵寇之时，中原用武，诸祖又皆敏有材力，习战尚勇，骑射格鲑，豪于乡里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159807_comment'></div>赵将军者，钜盗也，众数千人，张旗鸣鼓，攻掠郡县，其锋甚盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159807_comment'></div>尝过吾里中，不敢为力，遣使乞具一饭，诸祖诺之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159807_comment'></div>行人更其辞，贼愤，乃来战，遂阵于南门之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159807_comment'></div>我不素备，犹杀贼数百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159807_comment'></div>方战时，遇力疲则憩于门内，苏而复战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159807_comment'></div>贼势已抑，将引去未得，尚酣战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159807_comment'></div>三曾祖鞋系断，投门，门内有癚，闭门不纳，遂败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159807_comment'></div>是以长曾祖、七曾祖、大祖父、二祖父、四祖父、七祖父皆没于阵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159807_comment'></div>三曾祖善战，既败，贼入门，升堂阶，又斩贼<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>乃攀堂檐□□出里馀，息于栗林西数十步，渴就沟水饮，眼臶血出滴水上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159807_comment'></div>苦战如此，竟免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159807_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159807_comment'></div>石氏之迁，其当唐季乎，战之岁在晋开运三年也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159807_comment'></div>后五年，慕容氏反兖州，即周太祖广顺元年也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159807_comment'></div>贼后□□年，石氏乃分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159807_comment'></div>曾祖第六房无嗣，与第五房合为一院，凡六院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159807_comment'></div>后第四房嗣亦绝，为五院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159807_comment'></div>今第一院分六院，第二院分三院，第五院分四院，第七院分二院，合十六院，然皆出于七曾祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159807_comment'></div>□叙其略：第一院曾祖讳路坚，娶颜张单氏，生大祖父、二祖父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159807_comment'></div>大祖父娶秦氏，无子，女二人，长适西王张氏，次适南颜张丁让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159807_comment'></div>二祖父娶侯村郑氏，生长伯父明、二伯父静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159807_comment'></div>长伯父娶阳关朱氏，无嗣，一女适刘氏，湘、筠，其甥也<span class='inlineComment2'>（伯父□衋术，乡里名通传。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159807_comment'></div>二伯父娶淳于桑氏，生六男，曰用，曰诚，曰元吉，曰政，曰峰，曰宣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159807_comment'></div>三女，长适旧县陈隐，次适下村张氏，次适下村赵氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159807_comment'></div>用二男，曰峦，曰福；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159807_comment'></div>一女适聂氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1159807_comment'></div>福生圭，峦生先、得哥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1159807_comment'></div>先生大眼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1159807_comment'></div>诚一男，曰澡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1159807_comment'></div>三女，适寇氏、郝氏、韩氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1159807_comment'></div>澡生翁儿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1159807_comment'></div>元吉一男，曰涧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1159807_comment'></div>一女适夏氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1159807_comment'></div>涧生王儿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1159807_comment'></div>政一男，曰简；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1159807_comment'></div>二女，适周氏、李氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1159807_comment'></div>简生□。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1159807_comment'></div>峰三男，曰友谅，曰友直，曰友□；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1159807_comment'></div>二女，皆适张氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1159807_comment'></div>宣三男，曰全，曰师恭，曰师让；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1159807_comment'></div>二女，长适富氏，次在室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1159807_comment'></div>第二院曾祖讳路钊，娶刘氏，生四祖父洪、十一祖父瑰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1159807_comment'></div>一女，适李氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1159807_comment'></div>□□□□□□□□伯父□。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1159807_comment'></div>三伯父娶李氏，二男，曰坦，曰荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1159807_comment'></div>一女，适□氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1159807_comment'></div>坦生师睦、师和、师厚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1159807_comment'></div>一女，适晏氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1159807_comment'></div>师睦生课儿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1159807_comment'></div>荣生师哲、师敏<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1159807_comment'></div>十一祖父娶西张戴氏，生四伯父匀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1159807_comment'></div>二女适刘氏、张氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1159807_comment'></div>四伯父娶神氏，生宽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1159807_comment'></div>宽生修己、黑牛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1159807_comment'></div>一女，适成氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1159807_comment'></div>修己生扬七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1159807_comment'></div>第三院曾祖讳路宾，娶乾封黄氏，生九祖父文杲、十四祖父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1159807_comment'></div>九祖父娶屈沟□氏，生八叔父谦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1159807_comment'></div>二女，适耿氏、葛氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1159807_comment'></div>八叔父娶下村马氏，一男曰亨，二女适丁氏、刘九皋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1159807_comment'></div>十四祖父无子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1159807_comment'></div>第四院曾祖讳路珀，娶赵氏，事安太□师、赵侍中、慕容相公、索太保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1159807_comment'></div>天福七年补衙前子弟，九年补猎务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1159807_comment'></div>□□三年补中府猎射务都头。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1159807_comment'></div>乾皊三年、广顺三年为讨击副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1159807_comment'></div>无嗣，一女适戚澄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1159807_comment'></div>第五院曾祖讳路真，娶柏子赵氏，生十二祖父钦，一女适太子中舍刘阅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1159807_comment'></div>十二祖父娶南王王氏，生我烈考及仲父跻、仲父扆、季父居化；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1159807_comment'></div>二女，适西朱刘氏、柏子赵氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1159807_comment'></div>我曾祖笃勤农，乐田野，终身不游市郭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1159807_comment'></div>然喜衣冠，尝嘱我烈考于乡先生，愿授以经，因语人曰：「吾不取□，吾□金紫，□乡党，以儒名吾家，吾老死足矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1159807_comment'></div>烈考果登第，列东宫官，如其志<span class='inlineComment2'>（先是乡人以曾祖行呼吾家。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1159807_comment'></div>祖父，乡里称长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1159807_comment'></div>乡人乏，必贷之，果知其不能偿，即取券焚之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1159807_comment'></div>善处乡党，恂恂然无竞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1159807_comment'></div>今吾院视他院稍益，二祖之德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1159807_comment'></div>我烈考讳丙，娶郭夫人、马夫人、刘夫人、杨夫人、后刘夫人，专三家《春秋》学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1159807_comment'></div>大中祥符五年，真宗章圣皇帝御前擢第，仕至太子中舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1159807_comment'></div>生我兄慎齐及介、企、会、合与吾姊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1159807_comment'></div>吾姊适举子孙周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1159807_comment'></div>吾兄生师愚、师道、师勖、师诲、师默；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1159807_comment'></div>生女三人，长适进士姜睶，次适进士高枢，□在室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1159807_comment'></div>介生彭哥、川哥、徕哥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1159807_comment'></div>女二人，俱幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1159807_comment'></div>企生师廉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1159807_comment'></div>女三人，俱未嫁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1159807_comment'></div>会与合未娶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1159807_comment'></div>师愚生鼎孙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1159807_comment'></div>女一人，方四岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1159807_comment'></div>二仲父娶颜谢段氏，生屺、怀玉、怀德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1159807_comment'></div>女一人，适举子郭师颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1159807_comment'></div>屺三女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1159807_comment'></div>怀玉生师恪、师贤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1159807_comment'></div>一女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1159807_comment'></div>怀德生师果、师毅、师□、伯惜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1159807_comment'></div>二女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1159807_comment'></div>三叔父娶阳关薛氏，女二人，长适申村姜文，次适进士卢淑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1159807_comment'></div>姜甥铭、铎、锡、社哥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1159807_comment'></div>女二人，一适进士孙廓，一在室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1159807_comment'></div>二婿擅文辞，甥皆学，不为无后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1159807_comment'></div>四叔父娶申村姜氏、□高唐氏，生佥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1159807_comment'></div>女二人，长适王氏，次适任氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1159807_comment'></div>第六院曾祖讳□，娶杨氏，无嗣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1159807_comment'></div>女二人，长适西张鞠□，次适大吴刘□。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1159807_comment'></div>第七院曾祖讳□，娶戚氏，生八祖父文密、十祖父文秀、十三祖父；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1159807_comment'></div>女二人，长适石固王氏，次适颜谢商氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1159807_comment'></div>八祖父娶□氏，生五伯父遂、九叔父庆、十二叔父、十三叔父、十四叔父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1159807_comment'></div>五伯父娶乾封寇氏，生□□□□□；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1159807_comment'></div>四女，适王氏、杨氏、冯氏、杜氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1159807_comment'></div>九叔父娶大吴吴氏，生士元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1159807_comment'></div>十二叔父娶刘氏，二女适张氏、王氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1159807_comment'></div>高祖之五女，长适颜张许氏，次适乾封张氏，次适上高郭氏，次适侯村□氏，次适临□翁氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1159807_comment'></div>石氏始祖一人，高祖一人，曾祖七人，王父十人，诸考十四人，吾辈二十一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1159807_comment'></div>自我而下，诜诜未见其止也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1159807_comment'></div>若作厥室，始祖基之，高祖堂之，曾祖构之，王父丹之，诸考落成之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1159807_comment'></div>吾辈歌于下，饮食于下，于于如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1159807_comment'></div>然不敢怠逸，谨保堂构而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1159807_comment'></div>吾劄子若孙，既材而孝，其必能大石氏，基斯厚矣，堂斯峻矣，构斯崇矣，石氏斯传万世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1159807_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1159807_comment'></div>石氏食此田百有五十年矣，葬此地九十有年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1159807_comment'></div>自始祖至圭八世，能不失故田，能奉祭祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1159807_comment'></div>今举曾王父而降为三十二坟，用康定二年辛巳八月丁丑八日甲申归于大茔，以附始祖、高祖、曾祖，岁时则与十六院大合祭焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1159807_comment'></div>《诗》曰：「孝子不匮」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1159807_comment'></div>又曰：「无忝尔祖」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1159807_comment'></div>《语》曰：「死，葬之以礼，祭之以礼」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1159807_comment'></div>石氏子孙其庶几矣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1159807_comment'></div>茔域南北长四百八尺，东西广三百六十尺，合一十七亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1159807_comment'></div>大□一百三十株，鉵树一千七百五十株，合一千八百八十株。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1159807_comment'></div>石氏子孙贤也，茔阙固焉，宅兆安焉，树植茂焉，祭祀时焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1159807_comment'></div>茍不肖也，何所不至，戒哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1159807_comment'></div>□□□□□□□□德郎、守大理寺丞、新授通判通州军州兼管内劝农事、借绯士建仲书，承奉郎、待制、将作监主簿□颜辅篆额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1159807_comment'></div>孙湛刻<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_152_1159807'></div><div id='poem_sentence_152_1159807_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1159807'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_30_1159807_0'>⑴ □贼□□□□□头。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_70_1159807_1'>⑵ 四祖父尝为桑令公厅头，故乡人呼□龙。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_152_1159807_0'>⑶ 《金石续编》卷一四。又见陈校本附录佚文。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1159807_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年10月9日</a>　作《宣化军新桥记》<div id='poem_1159796' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159796' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159796?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宣化军新桥记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年10月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_1159796")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159796_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159796'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159796'>康定二年冬十月戊午，宣化军使、虞部员外郎张景云作清河桥成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159796_comment'></div>河初不通，故为之舟，则人利舟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159796_comment'></div>及其弊也，舟反害人，河不复通，故为之桥，救舟弊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159796_comment'></div>善哉，其达废也欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159796_comment'></div>圣人之于天下之道，有作焉，有因焉，有变焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159796_comment'></div>未有初也故作，未有制也故因，制失故变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159796_comment'></div>变者，救其失也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159796_comment'></div>汉董仲舒曰：「道者，万世无敝，非无敝也，得救之之道也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159796_comment'></div>毁舟为桥，善变者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159796_comment'></div>《易》曰：「通其变，使民不倦」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159796_comment'></div>其是之谓矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159796_comment'></div>河去军北门数步，其流不绝如线，深不濡轨，广不逾丈，非如彭蠡、洞庭之险，而人病涉则甚于彭蠡、洞庭，实舟之为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159796_comment'></div>舟有十五人，十五人为十五家，家率七口，为百五口，百五口之衣与食，皆取于舟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159796_comment'></div>晨起，十五家磨牙动吻，伸颈奋距，以博以噬，憧憧往来，人罕完肤，吁！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159796_comment'></div>上下相容，州县无政，孽苗遂威，癚府遂成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159796_comment'></div>凡此桥历二年，更六人，成辄坏者三，卒成于君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159796_comment'></div>如此其艰，孽苗大而难拔也，癚府固而难破也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159796_comment'></div>非君之诚与断，孰克哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159796_comment'></div>初，天章阁待制、知淄州军州事郭公劝，侍御史、京东转运使张公奎始谋毁舟建桥，授谋于县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159796_comment'></div>而郭以忧去，张徙河东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159796_comment'></div>其后虞部郎中胥君谷继来为州，国子博士霍君某通判州事，虞部员外郎韩君谷为县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159796_comment'></div>虽述六公之志，而桥再成辄再坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159796_comment'></div>逮君，桥卒成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159796_comment'></div>当二公之去、桥再坏也，人咸曰：「桥不可作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159796_comment'></div>物有数，事有会，兴废存诸时，成败系于天，皆不在人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159796_comment'></div>君来代韩，闻其说，独以为不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159796_comment'></div>茍兴废成败皆不在人，则救怀襄之患者，非禹也欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159796_comment'></div>定管、蔡之乱者，非周公也欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159796_comment'></div>平诸吕之难者，非勃也欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159796_comment'></div>去硉鱼之暴者，非吏部也欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159796_comment'></div>作一桥不能图久，人无诚也，乃推诸天，患诚不至，而不患功难就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159796_comment'></div>视事之日，亟至河上，且睵曰：州县之政，莫大于是者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159796_comment'></div>州之大者方千里，县之大者方百里，政之善恶不出千里之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159796_comment'></div>自西、自东、自南、自北，孰不由此涂出也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159796_comment'></div>苟有利焉，天下享之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159796_comment'></div>茍有害焉，天下被之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159796_comment'></div>在《周官》则曰：「司险，周知其山林川泽之阻而达其道路」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159796_comment'></div>在《孟子》则曰：「十月徒杠成，十一月舆梁成」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159796_comment'></div>在《春秋传》则曰：「启塞从时」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159796_comment'></div>癋二君谋于初，三君作于后，愿竭才卒成此桥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159796_comment'></div>且舟为害也远矣，吾为利也岂谋近哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159796_comment'></div>百世后已，不可茍作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159796_comment'></div>梓材以新，制度以侈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159796_comment'></div>夏六月己酉，明日落成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159796_comment'></div>其夕，桥又坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159796_comment'></div>君曰：「天固助予，非有奸，桥何坏？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159796_comment'></div>韩君再为桥，桥再为坏，坏有故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1159796_comment'></div>吾一为桥，桥一坏，坏于奸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1159796_comment'></div>吾未讨癚者，终成吾桥，然后信吾之志，而夺奸人之心，暴奸人之罪」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1159796_comment'></div>益勤不懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1159796_comment'></div>日出临河上，工之拙巧、材之良恶、斧斤之高下、绳墨之曲直，必亲焉，毋不良；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1159796_comment'></div>日入归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1159796_comment'></div>如此九十有七日，桥乃成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1159796_comment'></div>凡五杠、三十七柱、七十八梁，皆大木也，所以取大壮而图不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1159796_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1159796_comment'></div>衣乎舟、食乎舟者百有五，爪距森森，牙齿颜颜，相与横跂盘错于其间，崇奸深，树孽大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1159796_comment'></div>非君智果，奸府不破；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1159796_comment'></div>非君特达，孽苗不拔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1159796_comment'></div>始其再坏、三坏也，众口嚣嚣，咸请罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1159796_comment'></div>由于克断，君听不乱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1159796_comment'></div>由于克诚，此桥卒成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1159796_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1159796_comment'></div>君之功茂焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1159796_comment'></div>十月初九日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_63_1159796_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年11月17日</a>　于宅东北方建祭堂，作《祭堂记》<div id='poem_1159799' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159799' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159799?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年11月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_1159799")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159799_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159799'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159799'>周制：天子七庙，诸侯五庙，大夫三庙，适士一庙，庶人祭于寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159799_comment'></div>唐制：三品已上乃许立庙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159799_comment'></div>天宝十年，四品清官亦许立庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159799_comment'></div>介今官为节度掌书记，在国家官器令从七品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159799_comment'></div>说者谓：适士，上士也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159799_comment'></div>官师，中下士也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159799_comment'></div>庶人，府史之属也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159799_comment'></div>介为庶人，则尝命于天子，又未至于适士，其官师乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159799_comment'></div>在周制，得立一庙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159799_comment'></div>唐制，则未得立庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159799_comment'></div>今祭于寝，则介之烈考尝为东宫五品官，且鬼神之道，尚严于寝，实为黩神；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159799_comment'></div>将立庙，则介品贱，未应于式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159799_comment'></div>贵贱之位不可犯，求其中而自为之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159799_comment'></div>乃于宅东北位作堂三楹，以烈考及郭夫人、马夫人、刘夫人、杨夫人、后刘夫人居焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159799_comment'></div>荐新及于烈考五夫人而已，时祭则请皇考妣、王考妣咸坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159799_comment'></div>缘古礼而出新意也，推神道而本人情也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159799_comment'></div>庆历元年辛巳十一月十七日建<span class='inlineComment2'>（《徂徕石先生全集》卷一九。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159799_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1159799'>陈植锷校：「郭夫人」三字原无，据《石氏墓表》及后文「五夫人」补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1159799_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　作诗寄友人。作品：《寄元均》<div id='poem_83211' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_83211' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/83211?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄元均</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_83211")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_83211_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_83211'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_83211'>君为儒者岂知兵，何事欣随璧马行。<div id='poem_sentence_0_83211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_83211'>裴度樽前坐韩愈，赵成<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>帐下立荀卿。<div id='poem_sentence_1_83211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_83211'>御戎谁道全无策，对垒宁妨下一枰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_83211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_83211'>须信乾坤养不肖，年三十七卧柴荆。<div id='poem_sentence_3_83211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_83211'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_83211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_83211'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_83211_0'>⑴ 原作城，据石本、徐本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_83211_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年3月5日</a>　作《拜扫堂祭》<div id='poem_1159800' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159800' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159800?labeling=true' target='_blank'>拜扫堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年3月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_1159800")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159800_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159800'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159800'>石氏既用康定二年辛巳八月八日举大王父以下为三十二坟，葬于祖茔，复立祭堂于宅东北位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159800_comment'></div>葬之以礼，祭之以礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159800_comment'></div>石氏从周得姓逮于今，二千有馀年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159800_comment'></div>自沧徙居至于今，百五十有年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159800_comment'></div>祀远，唯介之烈考能谈其谱，讨源及流，实为详尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159800_comment'></div>小子尝受之烈考，终不有识，大惧坠落，又为石高五尺，广二尺三寸，厚一尺，列辞二千三百六十八字，表于墓前，以传千万世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159800_comment'></div>风雨燥眔，石久必泐，宇久必缺，不可无蔽覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159800_comment'></div>且岁时必上冢，出必告于墓，反拜于墓，则皆有祭，不可以无次设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159800_comment'></div>乃直茔前十四步为堂三楹，一以覆石，一以陈祭，总谓之拜扫堂云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159800_comment'></div>庆历二年壬午三月五日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1159800_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='d774cd402a8544a7a7b30d09f6c78a05_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d774cd402a8544a7a7b30d09f6c78a05");'><span id='d774cd402a8544a7a7b30d09f6c78a05_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>，41岁</div><div id='d774cd402a8544a7a7b30d09f6c78a05' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　通判濮州，待次于徂徕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年7月</a>　七月某日，病卒于家。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
晋中（榆次）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='330c22c09a774dc1ab44f5e28c6b851b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("330c22c09a774dc1ab44f5e28c6b851b");'><span id='330c22c09a774dc1ab44f5e28c6b851b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1029&endYear=1029')">1029年</a>，25岁</div><div id='330c22c09a774dc1ab44f5e28c6b851b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1029&endYear=1029')">1029年</a>　游历河朔，访柳开墓。作诗《过魏东郊》，缅怀柳开，对其推崇备至，至誉为“事业过皋夔，才能堪相辅”，“述作慕仲淹，文章肩韩愈”<div id='poem_83241' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_83241' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/83241?labeling=true' target='_blank'>过魏东郊</a><span class='authorDate'>（1029年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_83241")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_83241_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_83241'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_83241'>全魏地千里，雄大视区宇。<div id='poem_sentence_0_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_83241'>黄河为血脉，太行为筋膂。<div id='poem_sentence_1_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_83241'>地灵育圣贤，土厚含文<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>武。<div id='poem_sentence_2_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_83241'>堂堂柳先生，生下如猛虎。<div id='poem_sentence_3_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_83241'>十三断贼指，闻者皆震怖。<div id='poem_sentence_4_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_83241'>十七著野史，才俊淩迁固。<div id='poem_sentence_5_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_83241'>二十补亡书，辞深续尧禹。<div id='poem_sentence_6_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_83241'>六经皆自晓，不看注与疏。<div id='poem_sentence_7_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_83241'>述作慕仲淹，文章肩韩愈。<div id='poem_sentence_8_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_83241'>下唐二百年，先生固独步。<div id='poem_sentence_9_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_83241'>投篇动范杲，落笔惊王祜。<div id='poem_sentence_10_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_83241'>四方交豪杰，群公走声誉。<div id='poem_sentence_11_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_83241'>一上中高第，数年编士伍。<div id='poem_sentence_12_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_83241'>五命为御史，连出守方土。<div id='poem_sentence_13_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_83241'>事业过皋夔，才能堪相辅。<div id='poem_sentence_14_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_83241'>凤凰世不容，众鸟竞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_83241", 83241, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>嘲诉</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_15_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_83241'>狱中饥不死，特地生爪距。<div id='poem_sentence_16_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_83241'>貔貅十万师，盟津直北渡。<div id='poem_sentence_17_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_83241'>塞上诸猛将，低头若首鼠。<div id='poem_sentence_18_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_83241'>渴忆海为浆，饥思鳌为脯。<div id='poem_sentence_19_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_83241'>两手拿人肝，大床横牛肚。<div id='poem_sentence_20_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_83241'>一饮酒一石，贼来不怕惧。<div id='poem_sentence_21_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_83241'>帐下立孙吴，樽前坐伊吕。<div id='poem_sentence_22_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_83241'>笑谈韬钤閒，出入经纶务。<div id='poem_sentence_23_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_83241'>匈奴恨未灭，献策言可虏。<div id='poem_sentence_24_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_83241'>幽州恨未复，上书言可取。<div id='poem_sentence_25_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_83241'>好文有太宗，好武有太祖。<div id='poem_sentence_26_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_83241'>先生文武具，命兮竟不遇。<div id='poem_sentence_27_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_83241'>死来三十载，荒草盖坟墓。<div id='poem_sentence_28_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_83241'>四海无英雄，斯文失宗主。<div id='poem_sentence_29_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_83241'>竖子敢颠狂，黠戎敢慢侮。<div id='poem_sentence_30_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_83241'>我思柳先生，涕泪落如雨。<div id='poem_sentence_31_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_83241'>试过魏东郊，寒鸦啼老树。<div id='poem_sentence_32_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_83241'>丈夫肝胆丧，真儒魂魄去。<div id='poem_sentence_33_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_83241'>瓦石固无情，为我亦惨沮。<div id='poem_sentence_34_83241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
商丘
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e25ca239faf44976ba68b226feadae0b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e25ca239faf44976ba68b226feadae0b");'><span id='e25ca239faf44976ba68b226feadae0b_link'
