id='poem_sentence_13_83304_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_83304'>赫赫宋德，何有穷休<span class='inlineComment2'>（《圣文》三章，章十句）</span>。<span class='charType'>（三章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_1_83297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_83297'>隔在荒外，嗟尔并人。<span class='charType'>（一章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_2_83297_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_83297'>匪民之嚚，为贼俘虏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_83297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_83297'>往吊其民，王泽时雨。<div id='poem_sentence_4_83297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_83297'>往伐其罪，王师虎旅。<span class='charType'>（二章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_5_83297_comment'></div></div><br id='poem_sentence_7_83297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_83297'>并人望风，请为臣奴。<span class='charType'>（三章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_8_83297_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_83297'>旧是匈奴，为并左臂。<div id='poem_sentence_9_83297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_83297'>今附有德，不与贼子。<div id='poem_sentence_10_83297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_83297'>并人失恃，求就戮死。<span class='charType'>（四章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_11_83297_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_83297'>抚我则怀，并人肯来。<div id='poem_sentence_12_83297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_83308_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_83308'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_83308'>圣武惟扬，鹰师虎旅。<div id='poem_sentence_0_83308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_83308'>至于澶渊，执彼丑虏。<div id='poem_sentence_1_83308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_83308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_83308'>既俘其帅，请示死所。<span class='charType'>（一章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_4_83308_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_83308'>圣仁如天，恶杀好生。<div id='poem_sentence_5_83308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_83308'>于以耀德，匪来观兵。<div id='poem_sentence_6_83308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_83308'>亟命止戈，无兹黩刑。<div id='poem_sentence_7_83308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_83308'>千斯年兮，永以为好。<div id='poem_sentence_11_83308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_83308'>边人其安，养幼送老。<div id='poem_sentence_12_83308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_83308'>民有肥田，马有茂草。<div id='poem_sentence_13_83308_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_83326_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_83326'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_83326'>明肃惟母，实勤养抚。<div id='poem_sentence_0_83326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_83326'>有臣有虎，有离有附。<div id='poem_sentence_1_83326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_83326'>请王禄产，请庙考祖。<div id='poem_sentence_2_83326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_83326'>古人有作，规吕矩武。<span class='charType'>（一章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_3_83326_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_83326'>政在房帷，小人乘时。<div id='poem_sentence_4_83326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_83326'>十年于兹，惟几惟微。<div id='poem_sentence_5_83326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_83326'>圣人如天，不识不知。<div id='poem_sentence_6_83326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_83326'>龙晦其威，神藏其为。<span class='charType'>（二章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_7_83326_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_83326'>明道四月，睿德明发。<div id='poem_sentence_8_83326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_83326'>帝褰帘箔，出临轩榻。<div id='poem_sentence_9_83326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_83326'>总揽万机，指挥六合。<span class='charType'>（三章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_10_83326_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_83326'>圣人之兴，雷动乾行。<div id='poem_sentence_11_83326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_83326'>进退大臣，颜色和平。<div id='poem_sentence_12_83326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_83326'>诛逐群竖，左右不惊。<span class='charType'>（四章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_13_83326_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_83326'>不怒而威，不疾而速。<div id='poem_sentence_14_83326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_83326'>百蛮偷息，百官重足。<div id='poem_sentence_15_83326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_83326'>土无二主，惟辟作福。<span class='charType'>（五章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_16_83326_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_83326'>图任哲艾，拔崇贤能。<div id='poem_sentence_17_83326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_83326'>旌贲忠臣，死生光荣。<div id='poem_sentence_18_83326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_83326'>洗刷敝风，宫阙清明。<span class='charType'>（六章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_19_83326_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_83326'>惟帝之道，与时语默。<div id='poem_sentence_20_83326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_83326'>静则坤阖，动则乾辟。<span class='charType'>（七章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_21_83326_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_83326'>十年深宫，不有其权。<div id='poem_sentence_22_83326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_83326'>今日南面，退奸进贤。<span class='charType'>（八章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_23_83326_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_83326'>宋承大纪，八十年矣。<div id='poem_sentence_24_83326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_83326'>明道之政，独为粹美。<span class='charType'>（九章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_25_83326_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_83326'>唐三百年，时惟开元。<div id='poem_sentence_26_83326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_83326'>猗欤明道，开元同言。<span class='charType'>（十章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_27_83326_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_83326'>明道之政，可以歌舞。<div id='poem_sentence_28_83326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_83326'>小臣作颂，实惭吉甫<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<span class='charType'>（十一章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_29_83326_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_83326'></div><div id='poem_sentence_30_83326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_83326'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_29_83326_0'>⑴ 《明道》十一章，二章八句，四章六句，五章四句</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_83326_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年</a>　以《上范中丞书》，《上郭殿院书》，《上李杂端书》等表达其欣喜之情。<div id='poem_1159666' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159666' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159666?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上范中丞书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1033年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_1159666")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159666_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159666'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159666'>五月九日，郓州观察推官、将仕郎、试秘书省校书郎石介，闻新除中执法乘疾置趣归阙，且过于郓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159666_comment'></div>走短仆夫持书数幅，见长旄大旆至，则以书跪于马前，而宣其书中言曰：今天子命河阳旧相李公入平章中书事，命青州牧、天章阁待制范公为御史中丞，四海之望洽矣，三灵之心协矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159666_comment'></div>人主聪明，一朝独运于万机之上，沛然发乎宸虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159666_comment'></div>既已于四月十七日，天子宪法，行革近朝弊政七条事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159666_comment'></div>又于二十一日，罢八御药官，思扫除颓风，一新庶政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159666_comment'></div>乾坤上下，日月寰海，莫不清润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159666_comment'></div>乃躬引忠鲠亮直、恢闳博达之士，一立于珀廊，以出天下之政令；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159666_comment'></div>一领于中司，以持天下之纪纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159666_comment'></div>夫珀廊之上，政令所出，政令一不善，则天下无政令矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159666_comment'></div>中司之任，纪纲所在，纪纲一不正，则天下无纪纲矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159666_comment'></div>内外官府百馀局，唯中书、宪台为天子腹心耳目，为朝廷总领，为天下都会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159666_comment'></div>国家官人千数员，宰相、中丞执天子宪法，行天子诰命，布天子教化，故天子特重其任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159666_comment'></div>《周礼》有大宰、小宰，大宰则今之宰相也，小宰则今之中丞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159666_comment'></div>所以黄扉青琐，坐而论道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159666_comment'></div>绛服白简，会常专席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159666_comment'></div>盖以严其地也，尊其人也，示百寮不得而并也，众人不得而为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159666_comment'></div>惟主上英智神武，睿略雄断，能任人不疑，外取贤盓以自辅相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159666_comment'></div>惟相国耆德宿望，忠诚正气，能耐久不变，终升大辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159666_comment'></div>惟中丞大节直道，危言敢谏，能守正不挠，自结明主，简在帝心，符于物望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159666_comment'></div>人神上下，胥相协庆，穷天之垠，合亿万口，并亿万心，如一心，如一口，无人异辞者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159666_comment'></div>初，成命出，士走诸朝，吏走诸府，商走诸市，农夫走诸野，皓白之老，三尺之童，鼓舞欢欣，腾跃道路，曰：「天地久不序，阴阳久不和，风雨久不时，寒暑久不节，其待吾天子、吾相国、吾中丞而调乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159666_comment'></div>淫靡蠹人文，佛、老害政教，兴作夺农时，土木耗民财，其待吾天子、吾相国、吾中丞而救乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159666_comment'></div>刺史多轻授，县令多非人，良直多泥埋，奸赃多旌擢，其待吾天子、吾相国、吾中丞而辟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159666_comment'></div>中贵人党盛千馀年，口含天宪，手握王爵，出入内外，权倾四海，天子之命，不出于轩墀之上，而出于房闼，天下之政，不出于廊庙之间，而在于阉寺，其待吾天子、吾相国、吾中丞而禁乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159666_comment'></div>岁旱久不雨，螟虫久为灾，天下民阻饥而且将死，其待吾天子、吾相国、吾中丞而食乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159666_comment'></div>鳏寡茕独不能自养者，怯懦困穷不能自存者，闻之曰：「我其为吾天子、吾相国、吾中丞所生乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159666_comment'></div>穷海之隅，荒山之徼，覆盆之下，日月有不照临者，闻之曰：「我其为吾天子、吾相国、吾中丞所提乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159666_comment'></div>天子之明之圣，拟于尧、舜，侔于禹、汤，过于文、武，相国、中丞之功之德，格于皇天，被于四海，暨于草木虫鱼，故能感于人心，怀于民情，壮伟哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159666_comment'></div>以相国、中丞同德协心，左右我圣天子，天下太平，可延颈翘首而待也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159666_comment'></div>唐太宗得房、魏，明皇得姚、宋，故李唐十八世三百年，独贞观、开元为太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159666_comment'></div>以我圣天子，亦唐太宗、明皇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159666_comment'></div>以相国、中丞，亦太宗之房、魏，明皇之姚、宋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159666_comment'></div>岂知明道不为贞观、开元乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159666_comment'></div>阁下无曰：「吾位为中丞，致太平，宰相之事」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159666_comment'></div>阁下虽则中丞，天子之任阁下也，以宰相；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159666_comment'></div>天下之待阁下，以其中丞行宰相之事乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159666_comment'></div>癋主上注意，天下属心，践登公槐，正位珀廊，在旦暮矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159666_comment'></div>惟相国、中丞为天子、为天下致太平焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159666_comment'></div>且夫圣人乘运，运乘气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159666_comment'></div>天地间有正气，有邪气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159666_comment'></div>圣人生，乘天地正气，则为真运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159666_comment'></div>运气正，天地万物无不正者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159666_comment'></div>故其君为明君，臣为贤臣，民为良民，百物无札瘥夭伤，阴阳顺序，风雨时降，昆虫草木，各遂其生植，不有变怪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159666_comment'></div>盖至正之气行于天地间，东西南北，中央上下，无容发隙，妖孽惑邪之气无自入矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159666_comment'></div>有毛发之隙容邪气干之，正不纯一矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159666_comment'></div>故运气正，必有圣人乘之而王，圣人必有贤人起焉而辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159666_comment'></div>黄帝之六相，唐尧之舜、禹，有虞之十六相，汤之伊尹、仲虺，高宗之傅说，文王之太公、闳夭，成王之周公、召公，汉祖之萧、曹，光武之耿、邓，唐太宗之房、魏，明皇之姚、宋，宪宗之裴度，皆应期运而生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1159666_comment'></div>《易》曰：「同声相应，同气相求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1159666_comment'></div>水流眔，火就燥，云从龙，风从虎，圣人作而万物睹」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1159666_comment'></div>言各从其类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1159666_comment'></div>今天子乘正气而王，今相国、今中丞逢真运而生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1159666_comment'></div>圣贤符会，千载旦暮，在此时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1159666_comment'></div>惟相国不以十三四年处颠危困踬，变其前节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1159666_comment'></div>惟中丞不以三四年间取华涂显仕，塞其素量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1159666_comment'></div>直以得真主、逢真运，如舜、禹、十六相佐唐、虞，伊尹、傅说之佐汤、高宗，太公、闳夭、周公、召公之佐文、武、成王，房、魏、姚、宋、裴度之佐太宗、明皇、章武，俾我圣天子六五帝而四三皇，太平之基丕丕，与高天厚地而比崇永，三灵之心，四海之望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1159666_comment'></div>文中子曰：「君子之于帝制，并心一气而待也，倾耳而听，拭目而视」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1159666_comment'></div>太康之始，书同文，车同轨，君子曰「帝制可作矣」，而不克振；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1159666_comment'></div>太熙之后，而君子息心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1159666_comment'></div>今区域混一，文轸遐暨，圣天子春秋鼎盛，盛德日新，天下倾耳拭目，日以待尧、舜之治，斯亦常制可作之时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1159666_comment'></div>相国、中丞当竭王佐之才，罄忠臣之节，以副人主急太平之意，符天下倾耳拭目之望，无如太康之际，帝制遂不克振，使天下君子息心耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1159666_comment'></div>介生二十九年，在贫贱寒馁中，胸臆郁郁，不得舒散，一旦见圣人龙行雷动于六合之上，贤臣跃起云会，耳目如豁聋瞽，心意祛积滞，踊跃奋悚，不能制其喜，以笔尽写胸中事，布之于旌麾下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1159666_comment'></div>摈焉纳焉，惟命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1159666_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1159666_comment'></div>介顿首。</div><div id='poem_sentence_63_1159666_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年</a>　与举子士建中相识于郓州，对士建中甚为推重，引为同道。作品：《与士建中秀才书》<div id='poem_1159679' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159679' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159679?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与士建中秀才书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1033年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_1159679")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159679_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159679'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159679'>四月四日，徂徕石介谨致书士君茂才足下：洪水方割，下民其咨，禹乘四载，随山刊木，栉风沐雨，以安横流，以平九州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159679_comment'></div>武王既定祸乱，纣之馀民，疮瘠未合，周公践祚摄政，方一饭三吐哺，一沐三握发，下白屋之士，制礼作乐，以成太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159679_comment'></div>幽、厉失道，天下陵迟，孔子绝粮于陈，削迹于卫，伐树于宋，历聘七十国而不得用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159679_comment'></div>删《诗》、《书》，定《礼》、《乐》，赞《易》象，修《春秋》，以祖述尧、舜，宪章文、武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159679_comment'></div>斯三圣人，固已勤矣，固已劳矣，然而卒不惮者，息民患也，行圣道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159679_comment'></div>孔子既没，微言遂绝，杨、墨之徒，榛塞正路，孟子正人心，息邪说，距盶行，放淫辞，以辟杨、墨，说齐宣、梁惠王七国之君，以行仁义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159679_comment'></div>炎灵中歇，贼莽盗国，衣冠坠地，王道尽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159679_comment'></div>扬雄以一枝木扶之，著《太玄》五万言，以明天、地、人之道，作《法言》十三篇，以阐扬正教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159679_comment'></div>魏、晋迄陈、隋，帝王之道，扫地而无遗矣，生人之命遂绝而不救矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159679_comment'></div>文中子以太平之策十有二篇，干隋文帝，不遇，退居河、汾之间，续《诗》、《书》，正《礼》、《乐》，修《元经》，硈《易》道，九年而六经大就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159679_comment'></div>佛、老之教蠹于中国千百年矣，韩愈愤然于千百年下，孤力排毁，不避其死，论佛骨，贬潮州八千里，而志弥悫，守益坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159679_comment'></div>斯四贤者，亦已勤矣，亦已劳矣，然而卒不惮者，亦以息民患也，行圣道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159679_comment'></div>盖古圣贤方其天下未宁，生人未安，圣道未明，以谓职在于己，不敢安其居也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159679_comment'></div>方今正道缺坏，圣经隳离，淫文繁声，放于天下，佛、老妖怪诞妄之教，杨、墨汗漫不经之言，肆行于天地间，天子不禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159679_comment'></div>周公、孔子之道，孟轲、扬雄之文，危若缀旒之几绝，先生不救，吾徒岂得而安居乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159679_comment'></div>虽不逮古圣贤远矣，亦当穷精毕力而后已，庶几其道由吾徒而后粗存，犹愈于不为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159679_comment'></div>足下，生民之先觉者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159679_comment'></div>适水者，天下之人西而足下独东矣，盖沧海之所在也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159679_comment'></div>适山者，天下之人之秦之越而足下独之鲁矣，盖泰山之所处也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159679_comment'></div>适于东，须至于海，至于海，必涉其深，然后知水矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159679_comment'></div>之于鲁，须登泰山，登泰山，必穷其高，然后知山矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159679_comment'></div>适于东不至于海，如不东矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159679_comment'></div>至于海不涉其深，如不涉矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159679_comment'></div>至于鲁不登泰山，如不之鲁矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159679_comment'></div>登泰山不穷其高，如不登矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159679_comment'></div>癋其有中道而将止者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159679_comment'></div>介幸而不随天下之人之秦之越，而独随足下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159679_comment'></div>足下其援我手，我其蹑足下履，牵连挽引，庶能至焉，慎无为半涂而废者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159679_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159679_comment'></div>介再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1159679_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年</a>　秋，士建中中进士。介为之代郓州通判李若蒙草荐表，并为之致书枢密副使蔡齐等，多方延誉。作品：《代郓州通判李屯田荐士建中表》，《上蔡副枢书》，《上范思远书》<div id='poem_1159664' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159664' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159664?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代郓州通判李屯田荐士建中表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1033年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_1159664")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159664_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159664'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159664'>右，臣尝读《汉书》，每遇灾异，则诏三公、郡国各举贤良方正能直言极谏之士，上亲策问之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159664_comment'></div>故贾醓、晁错、公孙弘、董仲舒得以极其言，所以汉高昌言垂四百年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159664_comment'></div>今国家方惟新庶政，更修百度，日昃不食，急于太平，而蝗旱相乘，仍岁饥馑，朝廷忧劳哀痛，若内诸隍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159664_comment'></div>圣德日新，天灾未消，躬求谠言，庶闻其道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159664_comment'></div>臣窃见本州今秋得解建士士建中，能言天道人事之应，能叙三才九畴之义，能知太平之道，能息灾异之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159664_comment'></div>臣具见其实，辄敢荐明，惟朝廷策焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159664_comment'></div>伏以建中今三十六岁，专精毕力，劳心苦学，积二十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159664_comment'></div>性识通敏，经术深明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159664_comment'></div>读书不取其语辞，直以根本乎圣人之道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159664_comment'></div>为文不尚其浮华，直以宗树乎圣人之教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159664_comment'></div>故能言天地人之际，知帝皇王之道，通古今之术，识治乱之迹，怀经纶之略，有超异之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159664_comment'></div>其家至贫，养父母以孝闻，躬营甘旨，不避寒暑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159664_comment'></div>安贫守节，穷能益固，未尝以一介干非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159664_comment'></div>其人持身廉，操心平，睦乡里以仁，交朋友以忠，内守信义，外修操履，不以利动，不以妄进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159664_comment'></div>古之所谓经明、行修、文学、孝廉，建中实有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159664_comment'></div>昨秋赋时，本州考试得合格，已解发姓名，入礼部贡院去讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159664_comment'></div>窃以礼部每春就试进士，动有三二千人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159664_comment'></div>程式繁密，条制谨严，茍小有所误，便当遗落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159664_comment'></div>又与众人混试，复且糊名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159664_comment'></div>窃恐偶有所遗，则建中不得以名闻天子，其人遂不见用于圣朝，其道遂不得施于天下，文明之代，使贤者有不遇之睵，千载之下，朝廷有失贤之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159664_comment'></div>伏乞圣慈，更不送礼部试，特召令试策，访以王道之要，咨以当世之务，容其直言，毋讳有司，必有以补益国家者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159664_comment'></div>如其言可采，伏望圣慈特与收擢，稍不如举状，臣甘俟朝典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159664_comment'></div>干冒旒扆，臣无任激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1159664_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年</a>　孙奭以太子少傅致政归郓州，宴介等于私第。介亦有从学于孙奭之愿。孙奭归月余，于是年五月二十五日以病卒于家。临死命其子请介为其草遗表。介为之作《孙少傅致政小录》<div id='poem_1159801' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159801' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159801?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孙少傅致政小录</a><span class='authorDate'>（1033年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_1159801")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159801_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159801'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159801'>太子少傅乐安孙公致政归郓州，乡老故人从观于路，公马上色自得甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159801_comment'></div>三日，宴郡寮于私第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159801_comment'></div>乐半阕，起饮茶于致政堂，出真宗御制诗，上飞白书，客观拜舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159801_comment'></div>复坐，公顾客曰：「白公有言：『多少朱门锁空宅，主人到老不曾归』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159801_comment'></div>老夫今日归矣」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159801_comment'></div>喜动于外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159801_comment'></div>终食，客退，留通判张驾部舜元、观察推官石介，复于向所谓致政堂中，洁饣涤蒝，别陈酒张坐，与公乡里道旧款曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159801_comment'></div>仍顾介讽《易·离卦》九三《爻辞》，且曰：「乐以忘忧，自得小人之志；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159801_comment'></div>歌而鼓缶，不兴大耋之嗟」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159801_comment'></div>酒数行，公亲举令，命张和，诸孙皆立后，亦令继之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159801_comment'></div>曛夕，罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159801_comment'></div>明日，乘小驷，从诸孙游观北园，笑语絗絗，复终日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159801_comment'></div>即鮂召故人邻里，散金帛，皆厌其意，有宿负不还，悉复其券。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159801_comment'></div>月馀，公感疾笃，公谓子瑜曰：「吾无身后忧，诸经传中吾有未了者，此遗恨尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159801_comment'></div>初，公疾，辟暑居西厅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159801_comment'></div>一日晨起，忽索就正寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159801_comment'></div>明日，呼瑜及家人总至，公曰：「今五月二十四日也，辰在巳，明日当是时，吾终」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159801_comment'></div>因口占曰：「致政得请归，明道二年五月二十五日，启手足于正寝，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159801_comment'></div>是故君子谓之知命<span class='inlineComment2'>（上三十一字，公辞也。）</span>」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159801_comment'></div>复命瑜曰：「明日吾易箦之际，慎勿令妇人至吾所，唯汝与诸孙侍」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159801_comment'></div>因复慨然曰：「所贵不死于妇人之手乎<span class='inlineComment2'>（上十字，公之辞也。）</span>」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159801_comment'></div>又呼其婿范曙，谓曰：「不意便至于此，然死生有命，富贵在天，大数不足以介意<span class='inlineComment2'>（上二十二字，公之辞也。）</span>」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159801_comment'></div>又命瑜曰：「请石介草遗表，但叙平生感遇，勿复陈乞恩泽」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159801_comment'></div>瑜能行其治命，故瑜迁殿丞制云：「览遗奏之尽忠，故推恩而及嗣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159801_comment'></div>此梗鰖也，馀在国史。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1159801_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年</a>　在郓州观察推官任上。作品：《麦熟有感》（去年经春频肆赦），《宿村舍》<div id='poem_83246' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_83246' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/83246?labeling=true' target='_blank'>麦熟有感<span class='inlineComment2'>（癸酉中作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1033年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_83246")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_83246_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_83246'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_83246'>去年经春频肆赦，拜赦人忙走如马。<div id='poem_sentence_0_83246_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_83246'>五月不雨麦苗死，赦频不能活穷寡。<div id='poem_sentence_1_83246_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_83246'>今年经春无赦书，十日一雨及时下。<div id='poem_sentence_2_83246_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_83246'>五月麦熟人民饱，一麦胜如四度赦。<div id='poem_sentence_3_83246_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_83246'>吾愿吾君与吾相，调和阴阳活元化。<div id='poem_sentence_4_83246_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_83246'>阴阳无病元气和，风雨调顺苗多稼。<div id='poem_sentence_5_83246_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_83246'>使麦长熟人不饥，敢告吾君不须赦。<div id='poem_sentence_6_83246_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_83246'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_83246_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='0922a0a5cfc44435950bb4ff82c3644f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0922a0a5cfc44435950bb4ff82c3644f");'><span id='0922a0a5cfc44435950bb4ff82c3644f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>，34岁</div><div id='0922a0a5cfc44435950bb4ff82c3644f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>　作《题郓州学壁》文，赞王曾立学之贤。<div id='poem_1159789' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159789' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159789?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题郓州学壁</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_1159789")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159789_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159789'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159789'>沂公之贤，人不可及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159789_comment'></div>初罢相，知青州，为青州立学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159789_comment'></div>移魏，为魏立学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159789_comment'></div>再罢相，知郓州，为郓立学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159789_comment'></div>而罢相为三郡，建三学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159789_comment'></div>沂公之贤，人不可及！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159789_comment'></div>夫水之不涸，以其有源也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159789_comment'></div>木之不拔，以其有本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159789_comment'></div>学为教化之源，仁义之本欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159789_comment'></div>为国家浚源而殖本，公之心厚矣！</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1159789_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
四川（赴嘉州途中）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='5368b224c61040a0961619e75b8cfa02_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5368b224c61040a0961619e75b8cfa02");'><span id='5368b224c61040a0961619e75b8cfa02_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>，34岁</div><div id='5368b224c61040a0961619e75b8cfa02' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>南京秩满，以父年老，代父远官嘉州，遂任嘉州军事判官。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>赴蜀途中作大量即景咏怀及应酬赠答的诗歌。作品：《赴任嘉州嘉陵江泛舟》二首，《蜀道自勉》，《闻子规》，《赴任嘉州，初登栈道，寄题姜潜至之读易堂》，《士廷评相会梓州》，《初过潼关值雨》，《过温汤》，《过飞仙岭二首》，《蜀道中念亲有作》，《初过大散关马上作》，《泥溪驿中作嘉陵江自大散关与予相伴二十余程，至泥溪背予去，因有是作》，《柳池驿中作》<div id='poem_83256' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_83256' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/83256?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赴任嘉州嘉陵江泛舟<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_83256")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_83256_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_83256_0'>① 二首（二字原缺，据石本补），原本连作一首，此从石本、剑本</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_83256'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_83256'>中心横大江，两面叠青嶂。<div id='poem_sentence_0_83256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_83256'>江山相夹閒，何人事吟放。<div id='poem_sentence_1_83256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_83256'>半鐏岸帻坐，永日开舲望。<div id='poem_sentence_2_83256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_83256'>孤棹已夷犹，数峰更清尚。<div id='poem_sentence_3_83256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_83256'>危影倒波底，凝岚浮水上。<div id='poem_sentence_4_83256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_83256'>鸣鹭答猿啼，樵歌应渔唱。<div id='poem_sentence_5_83256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_83256'>并生泉石心，堪愧庸俗状。<div id='poem_sentence_6_83256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_83256'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_83256_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_83255' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_83255' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/83255?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_83255_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_83255'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_83255'>江心清照人，江面平如掌。<div id='poem_sentence_0_83255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_83255'>有客去逍遥，扁舟<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>浮荡漾。<div id='poem_sentence_1_83255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_83255'>远与城市绝，深将泉石向。<div id='poem_sentence_2_83255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_83255'>水鸟忽东西，溪云时下上。<div id='poem_sentence_3_83255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_83255'>轩冕谁富贵，琴鐏自闲放。<div id='poem_sentence_4_83255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_83255'>酒色照渌波，吟声入秋浪。<div id='poem_sentence_5_83255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_83255'>五湖何<span class='inlineComment2'>（石本、剑本作无）</span>范蠡，磻溪无吕望。<div id='poem_sentence_6_83255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_83255'>吾家徂徕下，汶水有清响。<div id='poem_sentence_7_83255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_83255'>常时夜雨急，随雨来枕上。<div id='poem_sentence_8_83255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_83255'>魂魄寒无寐，山居得真尚。<div id='poem_sentence_9_83255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_83255'>一为尘缨缚，不得闲时饷。<div id='poem_sentence_10_83255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_83255'>两耳聒欲聋，喧嚣千万状。<div id='poem_sentence_11_83255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_83255'>雨夜自潺湲，宦途空悲怆。<div id='poem_sentence_12_83255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_83255'>剑南四千里，地遐接蛮瘴。<div id='poem_sentence_13_83255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_83255'>乍听江水声<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作江声□，据石本、剑本补正）</span>，聊使心灵畅。<div id='poem_sentence_14_83255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_83255'></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_83255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_83255'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_83255_0'>⑴ 原作身，据石本、剑本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_83255_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
绵阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='05ddbf16a45a4bea834f5ee6254acffa_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("05ddbf16a45a4bea834f5ee6254acffa");'><span id='05ddbf16a45a4bea834f5ee6254acffa_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>，34岁</div><div id='05ddbf16a45a4bea834f5ee6254acffa' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>　赴蜀途中待阙左绵七十日，通判吕国博日相从吟酌。与睢阳之前任，现左绵知郡王虞部异地重逢，悲喜交集。作品：《赴任嘉州，待阙左绵七十日，通判吕国博日相从吟酌，至嘉阳，因成四韵寄之》，《左绵席上呈知郡王虞部》，《入蜀至左绵，路次水轩暂憩》<div id='poem_83204' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_83204' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/83204?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赴任嘉州待阙左绵七十日通判吕国博日相从吟酌至嘉阳因成四韵寄之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_83204")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_83204_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_83204'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_83204'>鼎来岂敢道能诗，一见何因便解颐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_83204_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_83204'>乡国三千里离别，杯盘七十日相知。<div id='poem_sentence_1_83204_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_83204'>送人江外马驮妓，垂钓寺中鱼竭池。<div id='poem_sentence_2_83204_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_83204'>别后中秋又重九，与谁赏月咏东篱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_83204_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_83204'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_83204_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
成都
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='96d6a220df424ee3825b95e64f97d0b1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("96d6a220df424ee3825b95e64f97d0b1");'><span id='96d6a220df424ee3825b95e64f97d0b1_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>，34岁</div><div id='96d6a220df424ee3825b95e64f97d0b1' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年8月</a>　八月十日至二十三日两到益州，共住九日。五次拜见益州知州张逸，张逸皆优礼待之。介临行之时，张逸借介舟揖，送其食物。作品：《谢益州张密学启》<div id='poem_1159708' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159708' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159708?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢益州张密学启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_1159708")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159708_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159708'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159708'>右，介启：介自八月十日至二十三日两到府城，共住九日，五次伏谒旌下，赐食华亭寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159708_comment'></div>每请见，皆特优礼待，九日费公膳十一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159708_comment'></div>及来赴官守，而复远借舟楫，盛送饔饩，精米嘉面，醇酒肥肉，率皆丰馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159708_comment'></div>尽室九口，在舟四夕，日以餍饱，犹不尽三之一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159708_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159708_comment'></div>饮食虽礼之末，礼非饮食不将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159708_comment'></div>《记》曰：「礼始诸饮食」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159708_comment'></div>《易》曰：「物不可不养，故受之以需。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159708_comment'></div>需者，饮食之道也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159708_comment'></div>又曰：「颐，养正则吉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159708_comment'></div>天地养万物，圣人养贤以及万民，然则饮食岂其细欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159708_comment'></div>故膰肉不至而孔子行，醴酒不置而申公去，古人岂专于饮食哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159708_comment'></div>所以为礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159708_comment'></div>恭惟知府密学，望高中外，德服西南，出以甸定四方，入将陶宰万物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159708_comment'></div>上养君后必以道，道者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159708_comment'></div>忠信之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159708_comment'></div>不以道，则徒资口腹之欲，与饲众人何异哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159708_comment'></div>下养士类必以礼，礼者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159708_comment'></div>仁义之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159708_comment'></div>不以礼，则徒取豢肥之意，与畜犬豕何异哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159708_comment'></div>介所以拜赐以来，为荣且喜，非荣一鲐酒之旨，非喜一桉肉之味，盖知府密学养不肖以礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159708_comment'></div>又府从事尝以介小诗尘于几阁，密学俯为属和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159708_comment'></div>虽不获赐本，而亲奉玉音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159708_comment'></div>是何蒉桴土鼓之疏，辄邀《咸池》大章之作，斯又希世之幸而非常之荣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159708_comment'></div>以州县贱小吏见国大臣，以属郡下执事见大尹，自当畏汗恐视，趋走阶下，望尘而来，拜尘而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159708_comment'></div>何得集如矩步，以宾客礼进退，从容近坐，款密奉对，声什唱和，饮食絗絗，来有劳，去有送，处具室庐，行具舟楫，若僚友者焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159708_comment'></div>迥出素望，皆逾常夷，为荣且喜，不亦宜哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159708_comment'></div>密学既以礼养士，愿服劳厥官，夙夜勉勉，使卒无旷败，以报万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159708_comment'></div>此则小人以力养上之效也，敢勤而不怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159708_comment'></div>近瞻府城，邀阻旌戟，卑情无任恋恩荷德、激切依归之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1159708_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
乐山
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='60b2a679abf14693a901bdf512c783df_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("60b2a679abf14693a901bdf512c783df");'><span id='60b2a679abf14693a901bdf512c783df_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>，34岁</div><div id='60b2a679abf14693a901bdf512c783df' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年9月</a>　九月初，抵嘉州。介自南京留守推官循资为节度掌书记，由将仕郎超阶为朝奉郎。作品：《予自南京留守推官循资为掌书记，由将仕郎超阶为朝奉郎，得蜀嘉州友人相贺者，因答之》，《嘉州读邸报，见张叔文由御史台主簿改著作佐郎，依旧在台》，《嘉州寄左绵王虞部》，《燕支板，浣花笺寄合州徐文职方》<div id='poem_83160' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_83160' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/83160?labeling=true' target='_blank'>予自南京留守推官循资为掌书记由将仕郎超阶至朝奉郎得蜀嘉州友人相贺者因答之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_83160")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_83160_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_83160'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_83160'>一循资走五千里，四遇恩超十六阶。<div id='poem_sentence_0_83160_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_83160'>自顾非才已过分，谁言英俊尚沉埋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_83160_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_83160'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_83160_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>　致书颖州知府蔡齐，谢其箴规训诫。作品：《上颖州蔡侍郎书》<div id='poem_1159704' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159704' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159704?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上颍州蔡侍郎书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_1159704")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159704_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159704'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159704'>侍郎阁下：夫物生而性不齐，裁正物性者，天吏也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159704_comment'></div>人生而材不备，长育人材者，君宰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159704_comment'></div>裁正而后物性遂，故曲者、直者、酸者、辛者、仆者、立者，皆得其和，《易》曰「乾道变化，各正性命」是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159704_comment'></div>长育而后人材美，故刚者、柔者、暴者、舒者、急者，各得其中，《洪范》曰「会其有极，归其有极」是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159704_comment'></div>和谓之至道，中谓之大德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159704_comment'></div>中和，而天下之理得矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159704_comment'></div>如介者，正所谓不合其中，而不得其和者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159704_comment'></div>喜、怒、哀、乐未发谓之中，喜、怒、哀、乐之将生，必先几动焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159704_comment'></div>几者，动之微也，事之未兆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159704_comment'></div>当其几动之时，喜也、怒也、哀也、乐也，皆可观也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159704_comment'></div>是喜、怒、哀、乐合于中也，则就之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159704_comment'></div>是喜、怒、哀、乐不合于中也，则去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159704_comment'></div>有不善，知之于未兆之前而绝之，故发而皆中节也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159704_comment'></div>《易》曰：「吉之先见」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159704_comment'></div>不言凶而言吉者，其能知善不善于几微之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159704_comment'></div>善则行之，不善则改之，凶何由而至也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159704_comment'></div>介见天下之有未得其治，则愤闷发于内，而言语形于外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159704_comment'></div>已暴著于外，犹不知协于中邪，秸于事邪，欲其吉之先见，发而皆中节，其可得乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159704_comment'></div>故凶、悔、吝常随之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159704_comment'></div>冬集至阙下，有人密道阁下之语于介者，箴规训诫，丁宁切至，如听箕子「皇极」之义，若闻孔思《中庸》之篇，释然大觉前日之非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159704_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159704_comment'></div>天以刚方直烈之性授于介，不纳介于中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159704_comment'></div>夫刚方直烈，不以中辅之，暴残戕折，日可待矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159704_comment'></div>今阁下驱介归之于中，是天以刚方直烈付于介，阁下纳之令德也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159704_comment'></div>天欲暴残戕折于介，而阁下赐之更生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159704_comment'></div>介荷阁下仁育陶宰，为至厚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159704_comment'></div>今西走蜀四千里，不敢以跋涉为劳，以平生未得一登阁下之门为恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159704_comment'></div>引首南望，不胜拳拳之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159704_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159704_comment'></div>介再拜。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_1159704'></div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1159704_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>　仿唐吴兢《贞观政要》作《三朝圣政录》。韩琦为其作序，赞介奉上爱君之心。<div id='poem_1159722' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159722' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159722?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三朝圣政录序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_1159722")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159722_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159722'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159722'>今天下太平八十年，物遂其生，人乐其业，我太祖、太宗、真宗忧勤养理之功欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159722_comment'></div>唐自天宝迄于天皊，百五十年间，禄山、朱泚、黄巢、秦宗权相接为寇，中原扰乱，生民荼苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159722_comment'></div>篡唐者非有拯溺拨乱之心，残暴愈甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159722_comment'></div>连绵五代，干戈日寻，戎马生郊，战血流野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159722_comment'></div>继唐终周，天下涂炭，实二百年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159722_comment'></div>我太祖武皇帝受禅之五月，诛李筠于潞州；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159722_comment'></div>十一月，杀李重进于扬州；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159722_comment'></div>四年，取荆渚，下湖南；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159722_comment'></div>六年，平蜀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159722_comment'></div>又六年，收广州；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159722_comment'></div>又四年，定江南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159722_comment'></div>太宗文皇帝亦承天位，能绍先烈，南致淮海，北降并汾，蛮夷戎狄，震慑请贡，海内自此始一矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159722_comment'></div>则太平之业，二祖基焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159722_comment'></div>真宗章圣皇帝，于是成二祖之基，以格于可大；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159722_comment'></div>隆二祖之业，以臻乎富有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159722_comment'></div>礼乐文物，焕然而章明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159722_comment'></div>教化刑政，淳然而大和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159722_comment'></div>太祖作之，太宗述之，真宗继之，太平之业就矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159722_comment'></div>若太祖之英武，太宗之圣神，真宗之文明，授受承承，以兴太平，可谓跨唐而逾汉，驾商、周而登虞、夏者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159722_comment'></div>臣生三十四年，目不识干戈之事，耳不闻金革之声，惟是草茅之下、里闾之中，听田父农叟歌盳三圣之德，盈溢乎耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159722_comment'></div>及登仕路以来，时接蝲绅大夫语，其说三圣之政益详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159722_comment'></div>然三圣之德，三朝之政，国史载之备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159722_comment'></div>但臣以谓三圣致太平之要道，或虑国史纪之至繁，书之不精，圣人一日万几，不能鮂览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159722_comment'></div>唐史臣吴兢，尝为《贞观政要》，臣窃效之，作《三朝圣政录》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159722_comment'></div>且人之言圣人者，必曰尧、舜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159722_comment'></div>人之称治世者，必曰夏、商、周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159722_comment'></div>臣观太祖武皇帝之神武、太宗文皇帝之睿圣、真宗章圣皇帝之仁孝，岂复让于尧、舜乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159722_comment'></div>观建隆、开宝之平定，兴国、雍熙之乐康，至道、咸平之醇颊，岂复羡于夏、商、周乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159722_comment'></div>恭惟景祐钦文聪武圣神仁明孝德皇帝陛下，有太祖、太宗、真宗之资，则当法建隆、开宝、兴国、雍熙、至道、咸平之政，以阜万民，以继太平，以丕于三圣之光，以树乎万世之基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159722_comment'></div>伏惟陛下聪明神圣，皆自天纵，言语动作，暗与理合，虽不师于古，不法乎今，固已高视轩、农，远超羲、昊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159722_comment'></div>茍更能斟酌祖宗垂宪，效而行之，可谓《韶》尽美矣，又尽善也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159722_comment'></div>伏惟圣主留意。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1159722_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
开封
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='39bf95bce40d4f2f9e057971b8fc93cb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("39bf95bce40d4f2f9e057971b8fc93cb");'><span id='39bf95bce40d4f2f9e057971b8fc93cb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1044')">1042-1044年</a>，38-40岁</div><div id='39bf95bce40d4f2f9e057971b8fc93cb' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>　服除，召入国子监直讲。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>　作《明隐》，言孙复非隐者，欲荐之于朝。<div id='poem_1159753' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159753' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159753?labeling=true' target='_blank'>明隐</a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_1159753")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159753_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159753'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159753'>孙明复先生，学周公、孔子之道而明之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159753_comment'></div>周、孔之道，非独善一身而兼利天下者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159753_comment'></div>先生畜周、孔之道于其身，茍畜而不施，徒自膏润肥硕而已，万物则悴枯瘠病，而自膏润肥硕，岂周公、孔子之道也欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159753_comment'></div>是以先生凡四举进士，则是先生非茍蓄其道以膏润肥硕于其身，将以利天下也，润万物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159753_comment'></div>四举而不得一官，鬓发皆皓白，乃退而筑居于泰山之阳，聚徒著书，种竹树果，盖有所待也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159753_comment'></div>且以谓尧、舜在上，必不使贤人布褐而糟糠乾饿以死，兹先生有所待之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159753_comment'></div>《礼》曰：「君子居易以俟命」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159753_comment'></div>斯之谓欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159753_comment'></div>世之浮近辈不达先生之心，谓先生隐尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159753_comment'></div>又不达隐之义，隐者当毁面污身，杜门绝迹，与鸟兽麋鹿为群，裂衣冠，屏饮食，弃人事，去妻子，寒则衣葛，饥则茹草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159753_comment'></div>先生有一不如是，则相与谤诽喧喧，谓先生不得隐之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159753_comment'></div>且人道之大，莫大于继嗣，故圣人重之，父以继祖，子以继父，孙以继子，相继而万世不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159753_comment'></div>故宗庙常血食，而四时无废飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159753_comment'></div>古之圣人，莫如伏羲，莫如神农，莫如黄帝，莫如尧，莫如舜，莫如禹、汤、文、武、周公、孔子，兹十一圣人皆娶，所以重继嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159753_comment'></div>且圣人之道非他，人道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159753_comment'></div>人道非他，君臣也，父子也，夫妇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159753_comment'></div>不娶，则是灭父子也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159753_comment'></div>灭父子，则灭君臣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159753_comment'></div>夫妇、父子、君臣灭，则人道灭矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159753_comment'></div>先生娶，所谓道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159753_comment'></div>世之浮近者喧喧诽谤曰：「既隐矣，隐则不得有妻子，乃娶，先生于是汩道矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159753_comment'></div>吁！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159753_comment'></div>先生学周、孔者也，茍周公、孔子皆不娶，先生不娶可矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159753_comment'></div>而周公、孔子娶，先生何得而不娶也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159753_comment'></div>先生不娶，则是灭人道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159753_comment'></div>舜为大孝，告父则不得娶，不告父而娶，孟子是之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159753_comment'></div>舜，大圣人也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159753_comment'></div>孟子，大贤人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159753_comment'></div>舜娶，孟子言是，是一圣一贤，必非有差缪矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159753_comment'></div>彼浮近者，岂可与之言哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159753_comment'></div>古之贤人有隐者，皆避乱世而隐者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159753_comment'></div>若箕子隐于奴，吕望隐于钓，四皓先生隐于山，萧何隐于吏，韩信、樊哙隐于屠市，严君平隐于卜，隐以远害也，亦非如彼所谓隐者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159753_comment'></div>彼所谓隐者，有匹夫之志，守薆薆之节者所为也，圣人之所不与也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159753_comment'></div>孔子谓长沮、桀溺，则曰：「吾非斯人之徒欤」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159753_comment'></div>谓伯夷、叔齐、虞仲、夷逸、朱张、柳下惠、少连，则曰：「我则异于是，无可无不可」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159753_comment'></div>若先生者，有尼父之志，遭尧、舜之盛，未得进用，姑盘桓山谷以待时也，非隐者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159753_comment'></div>如说之筑于傅珀，公孙之牧于海上，阳城之居于中条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159753_comment'></div>说终相高宗，中兴于商；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159753_comment'></div>公孙终相武帝，丕光于汉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159753_comment'></div>城终起于唐，以谏诤显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159753_comment'></div>先生之道，无少于说，而过于公孙、城，它日圣君聘而用之，吾君轶高宗而登舜矣，先生舟鰗于巨川，而霖雨于旱岁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159753_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159753_comment'></div>先生岂真隐者哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1159753_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>　力振古道，以诱掖后进，敦奖风教为己任，学者从之甚众，太学由此益盛。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>　时有蜀生何群，介感其“只知有仁义，不知有寒饿”，遂馆于家，使弟子推其为学长。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>　有闽人黄晞，好读书，客游京师数十年不归，介闻其名，执古礼聘之，以补学职，晞固辞不就。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　由杜衍之荐拜太子中允。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年4月</a>　三月，吕夷简罢相，以杜衍代夏谏为枢密使。仁宗欲更天下弊事，而增置谏官，欧阳修，余靖，王素，蔡襄入选。韩琦，范仲淹入京为副使。介大喜，称此为盛世，歌颂是其职也，于四月作《庆历圣德颂》，以范仲淹，富弼为“大贤”，而以“大奸”直斥夏竦。颂且出，范仲淹曰:“为此怪鬼辈坏之也。”韩琦曰:“天下事不可如此必坏。”孙复闻之，亦曰:“子祸始于此矣。”<div id='poem_83295' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_83295' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/83295?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庆历圣德颂</a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29818, "北宋", "石介", "poem_title_83295")'>石介</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_83295_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_83295'>三月二十一日大昕，皇帝御紫宸殿，朝百官，相得象殊，拜竦枢密使，夷简以司徒归第。二十二日，制命昌朝参知政事，弼枢密副使。二十六日，敕除修靖素，并充谏官。四月八日，皇帝御紫宸殿，朝百官。衍枢密使，仲淹琦枢密副使，乃用御史中丞拱宸御史邈御史平谏官修靖十一疏，追竦枢密使敕。十三日敕，又除襄为谏官。天地人神，昆虫草木，无不飗喜。皇帝退奸进贤，发于至聪，动于至诚，奋于睿断，见于刚克，陟黜之明，赏罚之公也。上视汉魏隋唐五代，凡千五百年，其间非无圣神之主盛明之时，未有如此选人之精，得人之多，进人之速，用人之尽，实为希阔殊尤，旷绝盛事。在皇帝之德之功，为卓荦瑰伟神明魁大。古者，一云气之祥，一草木之异，一蹄角之怪，一羽毛之瑞，当时群臣犹且浓墨大字金头钿轴，以称述颂美时君功德，以为无前之休，丕天之绩。如仲淹弼，实为不世出之贤。求之于古，尧则夔龙，舜则稷契，周则闳散，汉则萧曹，唐则房魏，陛下有之。诸臣亦皆今天下之人望，为宰相谏官者，陛下尽用之。此比云气草木蹄角羽毛之瑞，万万不侔，岂可翻无歌诗雅颂，以播吾君之休声烈光神功圣德，刻于琬琰，流于金石，告于天地，奏于宗庙，存于万千年而无穷尽哉！臣实羞之。臣尝爱慕唐大儒韩愈为博士日，作元和圣德颂千二百言，使宪宗功德赫奕炜烨，昭于千古，至今观之，如在当日。陛下今日功德，无让宪宗。臣文学虽不逮韩愈，而亦官于太学，领博士职，歌诗硈颂，乃其职业。窃拟于愈，辄作庆历圣德颂一首，四言，凡九百六十字。文辞鄙俚，固不足以发扬臣子之心，亦欲使陛下功德赫奕炜烨，昭于千古，万千年后观之，如在今日也。臣不胜死罪。臣贱，无路以进，姑藏诸家，以待乐府之采焉。</div><div id='poem_preface_83295_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_83295'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_83295'>于维庆历，三年三月。<div id='poem_sentence_0_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_83295'>皇帝龙兴，徐出闱闼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_83295'>晨坐太极，昼开阊阖。<div id='poem_sentence_2_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_83295'>躬揽英贤，手锄奸蘖。<div id='poem_sentence_3_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_83295'>大声<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_83295", 83295, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>沨沨</span>，震摇六合。<div id='poem_sentence_4_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_83295'>如乾之动，如雷之发。<div id='poem_sentence_5_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_83295'>昆虫蹢躅，妖怪藏灭。<div id='poem_sentence_6_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_83295'>同明道初，天地<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_83295", 83295, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>嘉吉</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_83295'>初闻皇帝，戚然言曰。<div id='poem_sentence_8_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_83295'>予父予祖，付予大业。<div id='poem_sentence_9_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_83295'>予恐失坠，实赖辅弼。<div id='poem_sentence_10_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_83295'>汝得象殊，重慎徽密。<div id='poem_sentence_11_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_83295'>君相予久，予嘉君伐。<div id='poem_sentence_12_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_83295'>君仍相予，笙镛斯协。<div id='poem_sentence_13_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_83295'>昌朝儒者，学问该洽。<div id='poem_sentence_14_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_83295'>与予论政，傅以经术。<div id='poem_sentence_15_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_83295'>汝贰二相，庶绩咸秩。<div id='poem_sentence_16_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_83295'>惟汝仲淹，汝诚予察。<div id='poem_sentence_17_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_83295'>太后乘势，汤沸火热。<div id='poem_sentence_18_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_83295'>汝时小臣，危言嶪嶪。<div id='poem_sentence_19_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_83295'>为予司谏，正予门闑。<div id='poem_sentence_20_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_83295'>为予京兆，堲予谗说。<div id='poem_sentence_21_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_83295'>贼叛于夏，为<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>予式遏。<div id='poem_sentence_22_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_83295'>六月酷日，大冬积雪。<div id='poem_sentence_23_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_83295'>汝暑汝寒，同于士卒。<div id='poem_sentence_24_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_83295'>予闻辛酸，汝不告乏。<div id='poem_sentence_25_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_83295'>予晚得弼，予心弼悦。<div id='poem_sentence_26_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_83295'>弼每见予，无有私谒。<div id='poem_sentence_27_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_83295'>以道辅予，弼言深切。<div id='poem_sentence_28_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_83295'>予不尧舜，弼自笞罚。<div id='poem_sentence_29_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_83295'>谏官一年，奏疏满箧。<div id='poem_sentence_30_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_83295'>侍从<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_83295", 83295, "Clauses/62/Comments/0")'>周岁</span>，忠力尽竭。<div id='poem_sentence_31_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_83295'>契丹亡义，梼杌饕餮。<div id='poem_sentence_32_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_83295'>敢侮大国，其辞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_83295", 83295, "Clauses/67/Comments/0")'>慢悖</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_33_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_83295'>弼将予命，不畏不慑。<div id='poem_sentence_34_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_83295'>卒复旧好，民得<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_83295", 83295, "Clauses/71/Comments/0")'>食褐</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_35_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_83295'>沙碛万里，死生一节。<div id='poem_sentence_36_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_83295'>视弼之肤，霜剥风裂。<div id='poem_sentence_37_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_83295'>观弼之心，鍊金锻铁。<div id='poem_sentence_38_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_83295'>宠名大官，以酬劳渴。<div id='poem_sentence_39_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_83295'>弼辞不受，其志莫夺。<div id='poem_sentence_40_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_83295'>惟仲淹弼，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_83295", 83295, "Clauses/83/Comments/0")'>一夔一契</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_41_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_83295'>天实赉予，予其敢忽。<div id='poem_sentence_42_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_83295'>并来弼予，民无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_43_83295", 83295, "Clauses/87/Comments/0")'>瘥札</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_43_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_83295'>曰衍汝来，汝予黄发。<div id='poem_sentence_44_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_83295'>事予二纪，毛秃齿豁。<div id='poem_sentence_45_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_83295'>心如一兮，率履弗越。<div id='poem_sentence_46_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_47_83295'>遂长枢府，兵政毋蹶。<div id='poem_sentence_47_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_83295'>予早识琦，琦有奇骨。<div id='poem_sentence_48_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_83295'>其器魁櫑，岂视<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_49_83295", 83295, "Clauses/99/Comments/0")'>扂楔</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_49_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_50_83295'>其人浑朴，不施剞劂。<div id='poem_sentence_50_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_83295'>可属大事，敦厚如勃。<div id='poem_sentence_51_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_52_83295'>琦汝副衍，知人予哲。<div id='poem_sentence_52_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_53_83295'>惟脩惟靖，立朝巘巘。<div id='poem_sentence_53_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_54_83295'>言论磥砢，忠诚特达。<div id='poem_sentence_54_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_55_83295'>禄微身贱，其志不怯。<div id='poem_sentence_55_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_56_83295'>尝诋大臣，亟遭贬黜。<div id='poem_sentence_56_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_83295'>万里归来，刚气不折。<div id='poem_sentence_57_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_58_83295'>屡进直言，以补予阙。<div id='poem_sentence_58_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_59_83295'>素相之后，含忠履洁。<div id='poem_sentence_59_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_60_83295'>昔为御史，几叩予榻。<div id='poem_sentence_60_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_61_83295'>至今谏疏，在予箱匣。<div id='poem_sentence_61_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_62_83295'>襄虽小臣，名闻予彻。<div id='poem_sentence_62_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_83295'>亦尝献言，箴予之失。<div id='poem_sentence_63_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_64_83295'>刚守<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_64_83295", 83295, "Clauses/128/Comments/0")'>粹悫</span>，与脩俦匹。<div id='poem_sentence_64_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_65_83295'>并为谏官，正色在列。<div id='poem_sentence_65_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_66_83295'>予过汝言，无钳汝舌。<div id='poem_sentence_66_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_67_83295'>皇帝明圣，忠邪辨别。<div id='poem_sentence_67_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_68_83295'>举擢俊良，扫除妖魃。<div id='poem_sentence_68_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_69_83295'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_69_83295", 83295, "Clauses/138/Comments/0")'>众贤</span>之进，如茅斯拔。<div id='poem_sentence_69_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_70_83295'>大奸之去，如距斯脱。<div id='poem_sentence_70_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_71_83295'>上倚辅弼，司予调燮。<div id='poem_sentence_71_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_72_83295'>下赖谏诤，维予纪法。<div id='poem_sentence_72_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_73_83295'>左右正人，无有邪孽。<div id='poem_sentence_73_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_74_83295'>予望<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>太平，日不逾浃。<div id='poem_sentence_74_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_83295'>皇帝嗣位，二十二年。<div id='poem_sentence_75_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_76_83295'>神武不杀，其默如渊。<div id='poem_sentence_76_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_77_83295'>圣人不测，其动如<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>天。<div id='poem_sentence_77_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_78_83295'>赏罚在予，不失其权。<div id='poem_sentence_78_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_79_83295'>恭己南面，退奸进贤。<div id='poem_sentence_79_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_80_83295'>知贤不易，非明不得。<div id='poem_sentence_80_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_81_83295'>去邪惟难<span class='inlineComment2'>（石本、剑本作艰）</span>，惟断乃克。<div id='poem_sentence_81_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_82_83295'>明则不贰，断则不惑。<div id='poem_sentence_82_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_83_83295'>既明且断，惟皇之德。<div id='poem_sentence_83_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_84_83295'>群下踧踖，重足屏息。<div id='poem_sentence_84_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_85_83295'>交相告语，曰惟正直。<div id='poem_sentence_85_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_86_83295'>毋作侧僻，皇帝汝殛。<div id='poem_sentence_86_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_87_83295'>诸侯危慄，坠玉失舄。<div id='poem_sentence_87_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_88_83295'>交相告语，皇帝神明。<div id='poem_sentence_88_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_89_83295'>四时朝觐，谨脩臣职。<div id='poem_sentence_89_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_90_83295'>四夷走马，坠镫遗策。<div id='poem_sentence_90_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_91_83295'>交相告语，皇帝神武。<div id='poem_sentence_91_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_92_83295'>解兵脩贡，永为属国。<div id='poem_sentence_92_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_93_83295'>皇帝一举，群臣慑焉。<div id='poem_sentence_93_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_94_83295'>诸侯畏焉，四夷服焉。<div id='poem_sentence_94_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_95_83295'>臣愿陛下，寿万千年<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《徂徕石先生文集》卷一）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_95_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_96_83295'></div><div id='poem_sentence_96_83295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_83295'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_22_83295_0'>⑴ 原作往，据石本改</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_74_83295_0'>⑵ 原作望见，据石本、徐本改</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_77_83295_0'>⑶ 原作以，据《宋史》本传改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_83295_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年3月</a>　三月，以韩琦之荐，直集贤院兼国子监直讲。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　夏竦诬介为富弼撰废立诏草，富弼，范仲淹俱不自安，请出按边。介不自安，亦请外，得濮州通判。<br /></div>
